## рҹҸҒ MILESTONE SNAPSHOT вҖ” 2026-05-25 15:30 (post Wave 4.1 LANDED + Wave 4.2 LANDED + Wave 7.2 LANDED)

**CE COPY TEST = ULTIMATIVNO 1:1 LANDED.** 30B spinova / 3 SWID, **svi unutar 0.05 %** Excel target-a. Avg FS bonus, avg CE win FS, FS trigger 1 in 139.90 = Excel **EXACT (0.000 % О”)**.

**Math is solved problem.** Wave 4 (universal `slot-sim` + multi-game refactor) i Wave 5 (Math Compiler Vision sa SMT/Z3 solver-om) su sada strateЕЎki fokus.

**Boki vision** (formulisano 14:25): jedna komanda `slot-build <PAR.xlsx>` proizvodi playable slot game + cert paket. Math je deterministiДҚki вҖ” ne klasiДҚan AI; LLM samo za theme/skin/narrative layer.

**Kimi deep research** (14:20) potvrdio: NIKO u industriji nema DSL/compiler za slot math synthesis. SMT/Z3 NIJE primenjeno. Verifiable PAR provenance NE postoji. Greenfield opportunity od 10-100M EUR.

Smooth integrali: 35Г— speedup. ETA 2-3 dana, delivered za 1 sesiju. | Sobol stratification + radical_inverse | 2-3 dana вҶ’ **1 sesija** | вң… **LANDED** |

| 3 | W149 follow-up Compensated math UK AWP | opt-in | рҹҹў only if expanding to UK land-based AWP |

**OBRISANO** kao viЕЎe nije relevantno za core "PAR вҶ’ slot game" misiju:
- ~~TestU01 BigCrush / NIST 15 / PractRand 2ВівҒё external reports~~ вҖ” external infra zahtev, ne donosi vrednost za pipeline
- ~~GPU Metal end-to-end byte-parity~~ вҖ” CPU 5.6M spins/sec je veДҮ dovoljno za 30B/sat, GPU = premature optimization
- ~~PGO + BOLT pipeline~~ вҖ” veДҮ landed kao W242, hot path je near-optimal na baseline-u, finished

### рҹҡ« Anti-duplikat NOTE (lesson from W226 session)

**Pre nego ЕЎto kreneЕЎ na "next wave" вҖ” proveri da li je veДҮ landed!**
1. `git log --oneline -50` za poslednjih 50 commits
2. `git ls-files rust-sim/tests/ | grep w<NN>` za test files
3. `grep -nE "W<NN>" SLOT_ENGINE_MASTER_TODO.md` za TODO entry
4. **Daemon i druge sesije paralelno rade** вҖ” proveri uvek pre dupliciranja.

## рҹ”’ PROCESS RULE (Boki, 2026-05-15, **OBAVEZNO BEZ IZUZETKA**)

**UVEK:** ultimativno reЕЎenje вҶ’ ultimativna implementacija вҶ’ **ULTIMATIVNO DETALJAN QA implementiranog** вҶ’ fix svih bug-ova naД‘enih вҶ’ commit + push.

Ultimate QA checklist (svaki Wave, posle svake implementacije, bez pitanja):

1. **TS lint** вҖ” `npm run lint` (tsc --noEmit) вҶ’ 0 errors.
2. **TS test suite** вҖ” `npm test` вҶ’ 0 fail, baseline broj specs ne sme pasti.
3. **TS build** вҖ” `npm run build` вҶ’ clean.
4. **Rust build** вҖ” `cargo build --release` вҶ’ clean.
5. **Rust clippy** вҖ” `cargo clippy --lib -D warnings` вҶ’ 0 warnings.
6. **Rust test** вҖ” `cargo test --release` вҶ’ 0 fail.
7. **Reserved-terms scan** вҖ” `bash scripts/check-reserved-terms.sh --all` вҶ’ 0 violations.
8. **Integration smoke** вҖ” `npm run optimizer-reproductions` ili equivalent ako je modul taknut.
9. **Master_todo update** вҖ” flip вҡ пёҸ/вқҢ вҶ’ вң… sa landed-note (file paths, LOC, spec count).
10. **Commit + push** вҖ” sa Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus + detaljnim message-om.

Ako QA pronaД‘e bug вҖ” fix odmah u istom commit-u (ili odvojen "fix(WaveN QA): close N bugs" commit ako je manji refaktor). Nikada ne ostaviti bug nepokriven kao "drugi commit ДҮe popraviti".

Posledica (50:1 producer:consumer disbalans Г— 5 paralelnih procesa): V8 heap ekspandirao ~8 GB+ per proces Г— 5 = 40 GB rezidentne RAM-a na Mac-u sa 36 GB вҶ’ macOS swap вҶ’ SSD вҶ’ disk full вҶ’ UI freeze. 4 od 5 W218 transcript fajlova bili 0 bajtova (procesi pukli pre nego ЕЎto su STDOUT-im pisali). **FIX**: (a) `dumpStream` postao `async` sa `await new Promise(r => process.stdout.once('drain', r))` posle svake false-returning `write()`; single reusable Buffer (drain garantuje flush pre overwrite-a) вҖ” heap sada konstantan вүҲ 1 MiB regardless of dump size; (b) `practrand-fullsuite-run.sh` default BYTES_PER 64 GiB вҶ’ 4 GiB, default PARALLEL=0 (sequential), opt-in PARALLEL=1, pre-flight disk-space check (refuse if free < 4Г— peak RAM Г— N_backends), `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=512` per backend (hard cap). **ACCEPTANCE**: 256 MiB dump pod 128 MB heap cap вҶ’ peak RSS 31.5 MiB, 0 swaps, 0 I/O. ## рҹ’ј COMMERCIAL READINESS вҖ” ЕЎta fali za "potpisivanje sa Tier-1 operatorom"

> Konsolidovana lista koju Corti moЕҫe uvek da pokaЕҫe Boki-ju kao "sales-blockers". PojedinaДҚni tehniДҚki flipovi za svaku stavku Еҫive u svojim Faza-sekcijama dole; ova sekcija je samo agregat za prodajni razgovor.
>
> Sve stavke su veДҮ вҡ пёҸ negde u TODO-u вҖ” ovo je samo cross-link da Corti ne zaboravi ЕЎta da pomenuje kad Boki sledeДҮi put pita "ЕЎta joЕЎ fali pre prodaje?".

- вҡ пёҸвҶ’вң… partial **NIST SP 800-22 (15 testova) LIVE izveЕЎtaji landed (Wave 173)** вҖ” official sts-2.1.2 `assess` build + `--dump` driver + 5 parallel STS workdirs + per-row N-adjusted parser вҶ’ **5/5 backends pass 188/188 sub-tests** (`reports/rng/NIST_FULL_SUITE.md`, 10вҒё bits/backend). вҡ пёҸ TestU01 BigCrush (~8-12h/backend) + PractRand 2ВівҒё (~30 min/backend) joЕЎ operator-initiated вҶ’ vidi Faza 7.2.
- вң… **Windows-x64 PRNG parity gate** вҖ” `scripts/cross-platform-rng-parity.mjs` (~200 L) generiЕЎe SHA-256 nad 100K outputs Г— 5 backends (mulberry32/pcg64/xoshiro256ss/philox4x32/chacha20) sa seed=12345, compare against committed `reports/parity/CROSS_PLATFORM_GOLDEN.json`. Workflow `.github/workflows/cross-platform-rng-parity.yml` vrti 4-OS matrix (ubuntu-latest / macos-14 arm64 / macos-13 x64 / **windows-latest**) вҖ” every push to main + PR. Drift na bilo kojem OS-u = failed job = engine determinism claim broken. Vitest `tests/cross_platform_rng_parity.test.ts` (9 specs) replicira gauntlet in-process za local catch pre CI. *(Wave 48)*
- вҡ пёҸ **TS Stryker mutation score 85.38 % вҶ’ 95 %** + Rust `rng` 92.65 % вҶ’ 95 % вҖ” strengthening tests вң… na 27 surviving mutants u `analyzer.ts` (Wave 26); rerun Stryker satima вҶ’ vidi Faza 10.7.
- вң… **20 IMENOVANIH industry pattern-a** вҖ” `docs/INDUSTRY_PATTERN_CATALOG.md` mapira 20 vendor-neutral mehaniДҚkih patterns (P-001..P-020) na postojeДҮe 30 reference fixtures + acceptance proof (`scripts/industry-patterns-acceptance.mjs` 60/60 PASS). Catalog naming je clean-room (no TM/patent rizici); operator rebrand-uje za commercial release. *(Wave 46)*
- вң… **PAR sheet sample kit** za 20 generiДҚkih mehanika вҖ” `scripts/par-sample-kit-build.mjs` (~340 L) pakuje 20 PAR samples (json + pdf + CSV per sample) + MASTER.csv (20 rows Г— 38 cols) + USIF schema kopija + Industry Pattern Catalog + pattern-mapped INDEX.md + standalone README_FOR_MATHEMATICIAN.md + SHA-256 MANIFEST.txt + VERSION.txt u `dist/par-sample-kit/` + ZIP arhiv (~132 KB). Acceptance gate `scripts/par-sample-kit-acceptance.mjs` (~200 L) verifikuje **23/23 checks PASS** (structural completeness / SHA-256 manifest no-tamper / USIF schema 20/20 valid / CSV shape / pattern coverage 13/20 P-IDs direct / ZIP integrity). MatematiДҚar preuzima ZIP, otvara izvan repo-a, ДҚita README + INDEX, validira hash-eve, otvara JSON/PDF/CSV bilo kojim alatom вҖ” npm/cargo/git NIJE potreban. npm `par-sample-kit` + `par-sample-kit:verify`. *(Wave 47)*
- вң… **Sales demo skripta** вҖ” `scripts/sales-demo.mjs` (~615 L) **8-step** interactive demo: В§1-6 baseline (engine sanity 4 fixtures Г— 50K, determinizam isti seed dvaput, ПҮВІ 5 backends preview, 15-jurisdiction emit, Node vs Rust 10вҒ№ replay numbers, cert paper trail listing) + В§7 HSM Seed Bridge LIVE (3 epochs distinct + cluster isolation + multi-instance broadcast + RCT/APT health) + В§8 PAR Commitment LIVE (Merkle root + auditor PASS pristine + tamper-detection FAIL + RTP-drift FAIL + integrity check). **Runs in ~2.2s** na M3 Pro (quick mode) / target вүӨ 5 min full. CLI flags: `--quick` (10K spins), `--no-color`, `--step N` (1-8), `--json`. npm `sales-demo` / `sales-demo:quick`. *(Wave 30 вҖ” initial 6-step / Wave 42 `87859be` вҖ” extended sa В§7 HSM + В§8 PAR commitment LIVE proof of Wave 38+40 industry-firsts)*
- вң… **One-page commercial pitch dokument** вҖ” `docs/COMMERCIAL_PITCH.md` (~150 lines) za matematiДҚare/CTO/compliance officere: 3-reДҚenice value prop, comparison tabela (Playa/Vendor A/Pragmatic/Vendor D), cert paper trail listing svih reports/ artefakata, auditor Q&A map, "what's still gated honestly", commercial proposition. *(Wave 30)*

## рҹ”¬ KIMI DEEP AUDIT 2026-05-15 вҖ” Top-10 prioritized engine gaps

> Izvor: `docs/research/KIMI_AUDIT_2026-05-15.md` (commit `7a4ea2d`) вҖ” 9 paralelnih search sweep-ova preko regulator docs / akademskih radova / vendor patenata / forum leak-ova + dark-side intel, 25 cited izvora, depth=deep, 3-pass synthesis.
>
> **Headline**: Engine veДҮ prevazilazi vendor baseline (TSвҶ”Rust bit-exact, 15 jurisdikcija, zero-alloc kernel). Tri kljuДҚna gap-a do Tier-1 untouchable: (1) **statistical RNG batteries beyond NIST 800-22** (TestU01 BigCrush + PractRand 2вҒҙвҒё), (2) **differential fuzzing + metamorphic RTP invariants** preko jezika, (3) **arhitektonsko RNG hardening** (HSM entropy, SP 800-90B, FIPS 140-3).
>
> Industry-secret takeaway: "mathematically certified" je marketing вҖ” labs vrte 10M-1B spinova + source-code diff, ne formalne dokaze. Jedinstveni gambit koji niko ne ship-uje: **zk-SNARK PAR sheet commitment** per game (otvara EUR 1B+ trust diferencijal).

**Industry-fact bullets (sales-pitch ammunition iz Kimi report-a):**

- PractRand-ov autor naziva NIST SP 800-22 "*literally the worst test suite*" вҖ” TestU01 BigCrush (160 testova) + PractRand 2вҒҙвҒё catch ono ЕЎto NIST propuЕЎta (PractRand Forum 2019, MDPI Entropy 2024)
- "Certified" je spin-count theatre вҖ” GLI/BMM vrte 10B+ MC spinova + SHA-256 manifest, ne formalne dokaze (GLI-19 v3.0 2024, UKGC Testing Strategy 2018 "outcome-based not proof-based")
- Samo **3 vendor-a** imaju SP 800-90B entropy cert (Rambus 2021, AWS Graviton4 2025) вҖ” niko u slot industriji javno ne ispunjava FIPS 140-3 IG D.K continuous health tests
- Vendor C LCG iz Knuth ART OF CPU **se reverse-engineerovao na ~24 spinova** (Russian "Alex" tim, $250k/nedelja, Wired 2017) вҖ” Schneier: "trivially easy to fix sa bilo kojim CSPRNG" вҖ” legacy cabineti i dalje vulnerable
- Provably-fair sa zk-SNARK postoji za crash/dice (GammaStack 2026), **0 major slot vendor-a** (Vendor A/SG/Vendor C/Vendor D/Pragmatic) вҖ” EP4046329 patent (2023) otvara prostor incumbent-i nisu uzeli
- cargo-mutants je active u Rust (ThoughtWorks Radar 2026); **0 slot vendor-a** advertise mutation-tested math kernel вҖ” kombinacija sa diff-fuzzing + property-based = unique verifiability story

| 57 | `cec4dee` | **Crash-style multiplier-only corner case (Faza 12 вҡ пёҸвҶ’вң…)** вҖ” `src/features/crashMultiplier.ts` (~250 L) closed-form za fair-crash multiplier-only Еҫanr (non-reel). Math model standard (Cabot & Hannum 2002 ch. 12): bust multiplier B вҲј Pareto(Оұ=1, x_m = 1вҲ’HE), `S(M) = P(B вүҘ M) = (1вҲ’HE)/M` za M вүҘ 1, `F(M) = 1 вҲ’ S(M)`. **Key theorem**: RTP = 1 вҲ’ HE NEZAVISNO OD cash-out target M вҖ” verifikovano za 6 strategija (2x, 5x, 10x, 50x, 500x, 5000x), sve daju identical CF RTP = 0.99000. **Var[Y \| target M] = MВІВ·S вҲ’ (MВ·S)ВІ = MВІВ·SВ·(1вҲ’S)** raste sa M, **Пғ/Ој ratio** se penje od 1.01 (target=2) do 71.06 (target=5000) вҖ” RTP konstanta, variance eksplodira. Plus `solveCrashHouseStatistics()` za game-level: median bust = 2(1вҲ’HE), P(bust<2x) = (1+HE)/2, P(bust<10x) = 0.901, P(reach M_max) = (1вҲ’HE)/M_max, E[B_truncated] = (1вҲ’HE)В·ln(M_max/(1вҲ’HE))/(1 вҲ’ (1вҲ’HE)/M_max). MC reference `simulateCrashTarget()` koristi inverse-CDF FвҒ»В№(u) = (1вҲ’HE)/(1вҲ’u) (untruncated Pareto) sa clip-at-M_max, ЕЎto taДҚno reprodukuje S(M) = (1вҲ’HE)/M. 31 vitest specs (validation 4 + probSurvive 5 + RTP invariance 3 + variance 4 + house stats 5 + MC 4 + edges 3 + det 2). | 157 | `4fa605c` | рҹҺҜ **Session Bankroll Drawdown Analyzer вҖ” 50. Е ta je 1-in-N hourly bust frequency koju regulator oДҚekuje da disclose-ujemo?" **Closed form Inverse Gaussian (Wald) distribution** za П„_bust pri Ој<0: П„ ~ IG(Ој_IG=B/|Ој|, О»=BВІ/ПғВІ); density `f(t) = вҲҡ(О»/(2ПҖ tВі)) В· exp(вҲ’О»(t вҲ’ Ој_IG)ВІ/(2 Ој_IGВІ t))`; **CDF** `F(t) = ОҰ(вҲҡ(О»/t)В·(t/Ој вҲ’ 1)) + exp(2О»/Ој) В· ОҰ(вҲ’вҲҡ(О»/t)В·(t/Ој + 1))` (Chhikara-Folks 1989 two-term form). Moments: **E[П„] = B/\|Ој\|**, **Var[П„] = BВ·ПғВІ/\|Ој\|Ві**, **median = numerical bisection na IG CDF** (no closed form). **3 drift regime klasifikacije**: (1) **Ој < 0** (house edge) вҶ’ sure bust, P(П„<вҲһ)=1, E[П„] finite, IG distribution; (2) **Ој = 0** (fair) вҶ’ sure bust, no integrable mean, median = BВІ/(ПғВІВ·ОҰвҒ»В№(0.75)ВІ) closed form za driftless BM hitting; (3) **Ој > 0** (player edge) вҶ’ P(П„<вҲһ) = exp(вҲ’2B\|Ој\|/ПғВІ) < 1, finite-time bust prob via Bachelier reflection. Disclosure metrics: **medianMinutesToBust** (regulator-friendly time units), **expectedHoursPlayed**, **expectedLossPerHour** (deterministic mean rate \|Ој\|В·spinsPerHour), **survivalProbByHorizon grid** [1h, 2h, 4h, 8h] default, **oneInNHoursBust = 1/P(bust within 1h)** (regulator "1 in X" form), **expectedBankrollAfter1Hour** conditional vs unconditional. Per-cascade M_k linear (base+(kвҲ’1)В·step) ili geometric (baseВ·ratio^(kвҲ’1)). **Closed-form payout decomposition**: Y = ОЈ_{k=1..L} V_kВ·M_k, **`E[Y] = E[V] В· ОЈ_{k=1..вҲһ} M_k В· p^k`** (Wald-style via P(LвүҘk)=p^k). For geometric: baseВ·p/(1вҲ’rp) (converges iff rp<1, validation guard). **`Var[Y] = E[YВІ] вҲ’ E[Y]ВІ`** sa E[YВІ] = E[VВІ]В·ОЈ M_kВІВ·p^k + 2В·E[V]ВІВ·ОЈ_{j<k} M_jВ·M_kВ·p^k cross-term. Truncation cap (default 1000) sa probability remaining disclosure (p^capВ·p, near-zero for typical configs). Plus `simulateCascadeMultiplierChain()` MC sa mulberry32 + walk-until-empty. Distinct od **W86 Cascade Sequential Multiplier Pyramid** (DETERMINISTIC per-cascade ladder, ne conditional), **W89 Persistent Multiplier Accumulator** (Binomial drop-chain FS-only), **W102 Cluster Compound Variance** (NO multiplier ladder), **W114 Sticky Wild Countdown** (fixed N-spin lifetime, time-based ne win-based). **32 vitest specs**: validation 9 + chain length distrib 5 + multiplier ladder 2 + win value moments 2 + payout decomp 4 + truncation 2 + MC cross-val 3 + det 2 + industry 3 (Reactor Wilds p=0.6 linear, Token of Life geom 1.5, constant step=0 вҶ’ E[V]В·baseВ·E[L] verification). Convergence validation enforces rВ·p<1 for geometric. Portfolio runner extended 32 вҶ’ **33 solvers**, baseCfg E[Y]=5.11 CF vs 5.21 MC (rel 1.9% @ 50K spins). Compliance: UKGC RTS 14 (variance + max-mult), MGA PPD В§11.f (chain volatility), eCOGRA. - **Kod i moduli** za faze 0.1, 1.x, 2.x, 3.x, 4.x, 5, 5.5, 6, 6.7, 7, 7.5, 8, 8.5, 8.6, 9.1-9.4, 9.6-9.9, 10.1-10.7, 11.2, 11.3, 11.4, 11.5, 11.6, 11.7, 11.8, 11.9, 12 (mehanike), 13.1, 13.2, 13.3, 13.4, 13.5, 13.7, 13.9, 13.10, 14.1, 14.2 **postoje i commit-ovani**.

## рҹҺҜ FAZA 200 вҖ” FULL APP ROADMAP (Boki, 2026-05-18, **C-Level Vision iz W196 retrospektive**)

> **Trenutno stanje**: imamo **dva mozga** (TypeScript engine + Rust MC simulator) + **77 closed-form solvera** + **97 P-IDs catalog** + **5351 vitest specs** + **106 CI gates** + **operator-package bundle** + **PAR sample kit** + **frontend skelet**.
>
> **Cilj**: kompletno re-skin Vendor B iz "engine vendor" u "**full slot-game production platform**" вҖ” gde game designer otvara studio, drag-drop math, vidi RTP live, exportuje IR + symbol art + audio, deploy u jurisdikciju jednim klikom, regulator dobija ceo dossier automatski.
>
> Trenutno smo **~25% od full app** (mozak gotov, telo skoro celo nedostaje). 8 faza ispod pokrivaju ostatak.
>
> **Ne pravimo demo igre вҖ” pravimo platform na kome se prave igre.** Svaki Tier-1 operator (Vendor B, Vendor C, Vendor A, Konami) moЕҫe da je kupi i ship-uje 100+ titulova godiЕЎnje umesto 5-10.

### Е ta veДҮ IMAMO вң… (W181-W196 base)

| Layer | Status | What |
|---|---|---|
| **Math kernel** | вң… 77 solvers | Closed-form RTP, variance, percentile, jackpot prob za 16 Vendor B gap mehanika + 61 generiДҚkih |
| **IR format** | вң… USIF v1.0 | JSON Schema Draft 2020-12 + Merkle commit + HSM-signed PAR |
| **MC simulator** | вң… Rust + TS | Philox-based RNG, paralel, NUMA, cross-platform byte-parity |
| **CI fortress** | вң… 106 gates | TestU01-ready, NIST SP 800-22, ENT, SP 800-90B, ПҮВІ, KAT, mutation, parity |
| **Compliance gate** | вң… 15 jurisdikcija | UKGC RTS, MGA PPD, eCOGRA, AU NCPF, JP Pachislot, NIGC, EU GA 2024 |
| **Operator package** | вң… 153 fajla bundle | Full cert paper trail u tarball-u za one-click regulator submit |
| **Industry catalog** | вң… v2.63 (97 P-IDs) | Svaki industry pattern u tabeli sa math + diff od ostalih |
| **PAR Sample Kit** | вң… 20 samples | Standalone bundle za mathematician walkthrough (no repo needed) |
| **Frontend skelet** | вң… drop-IR demo | Drag-drop IR JSON вҶ’ view solver output (vrlo basic) |
| **Sales demo** | вң… scripts/sales-demo.mjs | One-button C-level pitch reproducer |

### Е ta TREBA da bude full app вҖ” 8 FAZA roadmap

---

### рҹҰҙ FAZA 200.0 вҖ” WALKING SKELETON MVP (Vertical Slice) вҖ” *(вң… CLOSED 2026-05-18, 1-day paralel sprint kompromituje 4.5 nedelja procenu)*

> **StrateЕЎka odluka (Boki, 2026-05-18)**: Pre nego ЕЎto krenemo da gradimo bilo koju 200.X fazu u ЕЎirinu, **pravi se TANAK end-to-end slice** kroz ceo stack вҖ” math вҶ’ builder UI вҶ’ renderer вҶ’ cert export вҖ” za **JEDNU JEDNOSTAVNU IGRU**. Tek kad slice radi end-to-end, WIDEN-uje se feature-by-feature.
>
> **ZaЕЎto NE "math first"**: math je veДҮ 95% gotov (77 solvera, 100% Vendor B coverage). Dalji solver work bez UI/renderer feedback-a = mrtav kod.
>
> **ZaЕЎto NE "sve odjednom big-bang"**: 8-12 meseci bez funkcionalnog demoa. Bug u math-u otkriДҮe se tek na samom kraju. PraktiДҚno najgori pristup za commercial timeline.
>
> **Walking skeleton answer**: 3-4 nedelje do **first live demo** вҖ” "drop config вҶ’ vidi slot maЕЎinu kako se vrti вҶ’ izvuci operator-package.zip". Posle toga svaki novi feature ide end-to-end kroz ceo stack u jednom wave-u.
>
> **Target slice**: **klasik 5Г—3 grid, 20 paylines, 3-of-a-kind paytable, no features** вҖ” minimal viable game. Cilj nije lepota nego dokaz da pipeline radi.
>
> **Test strategija (kontinuirano, NE na kraju)**:
> - Math layer: 5351 vitest spec + portfolio + acceptance вҖ” veДҮ postoji, samo odrЕҫavanje
> - Builder layer: Playwright e2e + unit testovi po komponenti (svaki commit)
> - Renderer layer: visual regression (Percy/Chromatic) + 60fps frame-rate budget guard
> - End-to-end: 1 reference IR вҶ’ builder import вҶ’ renderer spin вҶ’ cert export вҶ’ SVE u jednom test pipe-u

---

#### 200.0.1 вҖ” W197 STUDIO BUILDER UI SKELETON вқҢ *(3-5 dana, prvi sprint walking-skeleton-a)*

**Cilj**: Designer u browser-u napravi 5Г—3 igru kroz UI (bez JSON editora) i dobije live RTP estimate.

**Е to veДҮ postoji** (build-on): `web/studio.html` + `web/studio.js` (W152 Wave 26 imali Export/Import IR JSON + live spin preview).

**Nova implementacija**:
- **Reel editor komponenta** (`web/components/ReelEditor.{html,js,css}`) вҖ” vizuelna kolona po reel-u, drag-drop iz palette, klik-edit weight (0-100), real-time validation (reel coverage вүҘ 95%)
- **Symbol palette komponenta** (`web/components/SymbolPalette.{html,js,css}`) вҖ” 11 predefined slot simbola sa SVG ikonicama (9-10-J-Q-K-A high cards + 4 theme symbols + 1 WILD + 1 SCATTER), drag handler za reel cells
- **Paytable grid komponenta** (`web/components/PaytableGrid.{html,js,css}`) вҖ” sve simbole Г— {3-of, 4-of, 5-of} sa numeric input, color-coded by tier (high/mid/low), auto-sum validation
- **Topology selector** (`web/components/TopologySelector.{html,js}`) вҖ” drop-down: 3Г—3 / 5Г—3 / 5Г—4 / 6Г—4 / 7Г—7 (uses postojeДҮe `tests/fixtures/reference/*.json` kao defaults)
- **"Compute RTP" dugme** вҖ” debounced 100ms na svaki edit, poziva `src/calculator/rtpCalculator.ts` na in-memory IR object, prikazuje rezultat u side panel-u
- **Live PAR panel** (`web/components/LivePAR.{html,js,css}`) вҖ” RTP %, hit frequency %, per-symbol contribution chart (D3 ili Chart.js), volatility category (LOW/MED/HIGH bar)
- **IR Export dugme** вҖ” emits canonical JSON sa Merkle root (postojeДҮe `src/cert/`)
- **IR Import dugme** вҖ” drop JSON file вҶ’ populate sve komponente (round-trip test)

**QA gates W197**:
- вң… Playwright e2e: "create 5Г—3 game from scratch, set 20 paylines, fill paytable, see RTP within 5s"
- вң… Vitest unit: svaka komponenta 15-20 specs (input validation, state mutation, edge cases)
- вң… Round-trip test: import `tests/fixtures/reference/5x3-20lines.json` вҶ’ UI вҶ’ re-export вҶ’ byte-identical sa original
- вң… Visual regression: 6 baseline screenshots (empty / loaded / RTP computed / paytable edit / topology switch / IR export modal)
- вң… Performance: full RTP recompute < 100ms na M3 Pro za 5Г—3 grid
- вң… TS lint + build clean / 0 regresija na 5351 postojeДҮih vitest specs

**Commit + pin posle W197** (Cortex policy: nikad ne preskaДҚemo).

---

#### 200.0.2 вҖ” W198 WEBGL RENDERER MINIMAL вқҢ *(5-7 dana, drugi sprint walking-skeleton-a)*

**Cilj**: Builder IR JSON вҶ’ slot maЕЎina koja se VRTI u browser-u sa spin animacijom + win line draw. Bez audio, bez bonus, bez features.

**Tech stack**:
- **Pixi.js v8** (lightweight WebGL 2.0, dobar developer ergo za sprite-based slot maЕЎine, manji bundle od Phaser)
- Alternative considered: Phaser 3 (preteЕЎka za slot use case), raw WebGL (preskup engineering za walking skeleton)
- Pixi.js zakljuДҚno bere ako benchmark @ 60fps fails na low-end Chromebook

**Nova implementacija**:
- **Renderer paket** (`web/renderer/`):
  - `Renderer.ts` вҖ” bootstrap (Pixi.Application, stage setup, asset loader)
  - `ReelStrip.ts` вҖ” vertical scroll reel sa acceleration вҶ’ steady вҶ’ deceleration kinematics
  - `SymbolSprite.ts` вҖ” symbol tile sa idle/blur/win animacijama (3-frame minimal)
  - `WinLineRenderer.ts` вҖ” draw paylines on win (animated dash, fade-in/out, per-line color)
  - `SpinController.ts` вҖ” orchestrates 5 reels (sequential stop sa 100-200ms delay, anticipation pause na near-win)
  - `IRToRendererAdapter.ts` вҖ” IR JSON вҶ’ renderer config (reel strips вҶ’ symbol sequences, paytable вҶ’ win mapping)
- **Symbol asset pack** (`web/assets/symbols/`):
  - 11 SVG ikonice (originalni layout, theme: classic Vegas neon вҶ’ 9/10/J/Q/K/A + 4 theme fruits/jewels + WILD + SCATTER)
  - SVG вҶ’ PNG @ 128Г—128 + 256Г—256 (retina) atlas via build script
  - Audio placeholder (silent .ogg sa proper duration tags, audio ide u W199+)
- **Spin lifecycle**:
  1. Player klikne "SPIN" вҶ’ controller poziva `src/engine/spin.ts` sa current IR
  2. Engine returns spin result (stop positions per reel + win lines)
  3. Renderer animates reel spin (1.5-2.5s total, sequential stops sa anticipation)
  4. Win lines draw 1.5s posle final reel stop
  5. Spin again ready

**QA gates W198**:
- вң… Playwright e2e: "load 5Г—3-20lines IR вҶ’ click spin вҶ’ reels spin вҶ’ final position matches engine.spin() result"
- вң… Frame-rate budget: stable 60fps na M3 Pro + 30fps minimum na throttled Chromebook (CPU 4Г— slowdown)
- вң… Visual regression: 10 baseline frames (idle / spinning t=0/0.5/1.0/1.5s / stopped / win-line-1 / win-line-2 / win-all / fade-out)
- вң… Deterministic spin test: same seed вҶ’ identical visual outcome (frame hash compare)
- вң… Asset loader: 11 SVG sprites < 500ms total load on cold cache
- вң… Bundle size: full renderer + assets < 800KB gzipped
- вң… Memory: no leaks across 100 consecutive spins (Chrome DevTools snapshot diff)

**Commit + pin posle W198**.

---

#### 200.0.3 вҖ” W199 END-TO-END INTEGRATION + CERT EXPORT вқҢ *(3-5 dana, treДҮi sprint walking-skeleton-a)*

**Cilj**: Builder вҶ’ Renderer вҶ’ Cert export, sve u jednoj live demo sesiji. "Designer otvori studio, napravi igru, pusti spin, exportuje regulator package."

**Nova implementacija**:
- **Unified Studio app** (`web/studio.html` refactor) вҖ” single-page app sa 3 tab-a:
  - **Tab 1: BUILD** (W197 reel editor + paytable + topology + live PAR)
  - **Tab 2: PLAY** (W198 renderer sa "SPIN" / "AUTOPLAY 10" dugmiДҮima, credit balance, bet selector, spin history log)
  - **Tab 3: CERTIFY** (Monte Carlo runner + cert pipeline)
- **MC trigger button** u Tab 3 вҖ” pokreДҮe `npm run sim -- --config <IR>` preko webworker (ili WASM build Rust simulator-a za client-side MC) na 100K-1M spinova, progress bar + ETA
- **PAR Sheet preview** posle MC вҖ” 12 GLI-16 sekcija u tabovima (RTP / hit freq / volatility / quantiles / moments / bonus distances / required spins / compliance)
- **Operator package export** вҖ” klik "Download operator-package.zip" poziva `scripts/operator-package.sh` (postojeДҮi) i serves bundle iz browser-a
- **Jurisdiction picker** u export modalu вҖ” UKGC / MGA / ADM / eCOGRA / EU GA 2024 вҶ’ emits jurisdiction-specific overlay u package
- **Cross-tab state sync** вҖ” IR object u jedinstvenom store-u (Zustand ili plain reactive proxy), nikad ne gubi rad izmeД‘u tabova

**QA gates W199**:
- вң… Playwright e2e SCENARIO 1 (the demo): "Build 5Г—3-20-lines from blank вҶ’ spin 5 times u Play tab-u вҶ’ run 100K MC вҶ’ export operator-package.zip вҶ’ unzip вҶ’ manifest contains PAR + IR + Merkle + jurisdiction overlay"
- вң… Playwright e2e SCENARIO 2 (round-trip): "Import existing hnw-classic.json вҶ’ all 3 tabs populate correctly вҶ’ spin renders H&W placeholder (no animation yet, just text overlay) вҶ’ export вҶ’ re-import вҶ’ byte-identical"
- вң… Vitest e2e: full pipeline `IR вҶ’ calculator вҶ’ MC simulator вҶ’ PAR вҶ’ operator-package` u jednom test fajlu
- вң… Performance: tab switch < 50ms, MC 100K spins < 3s na M3 Pro
- вң… Operator package SHA-256 manifest: 100% match sa `scripts/operator-package.sh` reference output

**Commit + pin posle W199**.

---

#### 200.0.4 вҖ” W200 рҹҸҶ DEMO-READY MILESTONE + DOCUMENTATION вқҢ *(2-3 dana, walking-skeleton closure)*

**Cilj**: Walking skeleton je polished, demo-ready, sa video walkthrough + sales pitch.

**Nova implementacija**:
- **Polish pass** вҖ” UX cleanup, error messages, loading states, empty states (sve sa kojima C-level demo moЕҫe razbiti)
- **Demo script** (`scripts/walking-skeleton-demo.mjs`) вҖ” automated 3-minute live demo: open studio вҶ’ build game вҶ’ spin вҶ’ MC вҶ’ export, sa narration prompts za prezentera

- **Master TODO update** вҖ” W200 milestone row + Faza 200.0 вң… flip + sledeДҮih waveova roadmap (W201+ = Faza 200.1 Math Studio expansion / 200.2 Symbol Pipeline / 200.3 Runtime Engine вҖ” paralelno)

**QA gates W200**:
- вң… End-to-end demo runs < 3 minuta on first-time user (Boki ili tester)
- вң… Demo video uploaded i playable
- вң… COMMERCIAL_PITCH_v2.md sa screenshot-ima

## рҹҺҜ FAZA 200.0 IMPLEMENTACIJA вҖ” DETALJAN MICRO-PLAN (Boki, 2026-05-18, posle v5 mockup iteracija)

> **Kontekst**: posle 5 iteracija mockup-a (corti / kimi / v2-baseline / v2-engine / v3-dark-onyx / v3-dark-deep / v4-final / **v5-final-studio**) imamo locked baseline:
> - Onyx + cyan engineering paleta
> - 4-row shell (header / tabs / main / status), 6 tab-ova (BUILD / COMPOSE / CATALOG / PLAY / SENSITIVITY / CERTIFY)
> - Workspaces Г— Variants Г— Compare A/B
> - DinamiДҚki symbol pool (HP/MP/LP/Wild/Scatter/Mult sa auto-naming HP1, HP2... + per-symbol rename)
> - Context-aware right rail
> - вҢҳK command palette, kbd shortcuts
> - 40 cyan stroke SVG icon library
>
> **Lokacija mockup-a**: `web/mockups/v5-final-studio/` (336K, 4 fajla + 40 SVG)
> **Cilj implementacije**: pretvoriti mockup u **production app** sa real engine integracijom (postojeДҮa 77 closed-form solvera + 5351 vitest specs + Rust MC simulator + GLI-16 PAR + 15 jurisdiction profiles)
>
> **Strategy**: ne re-build u React/Vue/Svelte. Mockup je vanilla HTML/CSS/JS, brz, file:// safe, lakЕЎe integrisati direktno sa postojeДҮim TypeScript `src/` modulima (build-free via `<script type="module">` import). Ako kasnije treba framework вҖ” refactor je opt-in, ne mandatory.

### 200.0.0 вҖ” PRECONDITION POPRAVKE U v5 MOCKUPU (pre nego ЕЎto kreДҮe implementacija)

#### 200.0.0.A вҖ” Persona LAYOUT redesign (Boki feedback "koja je razlika"?) вқҢ
Trenutno: 2 CSS pravila + 1 div. To NIJE prava persona separacija.
Cilj: tri kompletno razliДҚita layout-a koja se prebacuju, jer Math/Design/Producer imaju razliДҚite workflow-e:

| Persona | Primary tab | Primary action | Side info | Headline metric |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **MATH** (default) | SENSITIVITY | Run sensitivity sweep | Пғ, P99, kurtosis, skew, Ој4 sa formulama | RTP 96.4214% (4dp) |
| **DESIGN** | PLAY | Spin preview + audio | Animation timeline + theme picker | "Win feel" tight/balanced/loose |
| **PRODUCER** | CERTIFY | Submit to regulator | KPI cards + 12-month roadmap | Days-to-cert + budget |

Promene:
- Math: 4dp precision, "View formula" links, Sensitivity slider primary, Catalog filter = math complexity
- Design: simboli Г—2.0 (ne 1.10), theme picker (Geological/Cosmic/Botanical/Mineral/Acoustic), "Win feel" indicator umesto numeriДҚkog RTP, audio cue toggle, Catalog filter = visual theme
- Producer: KPI strip prominent (cost saved $40K/title, time-to-cert 11d, regulator rejection 0%, releases/quarter 12), Submit to regulator big primary button, multi-game pipeline view, Catalog filter = jurisdiction + status

QA: Playwright 3 scenarios (Math user flow / Design user flow / Producer user flow), svaki sa razliДҚitim primary action expected na load.

### 200.0.1 вҖ” W197 STUDIO BUILDER UI SKELETON (REAL ENGINE WIRING) вқҢ

**Nije viЕЎe mockup вҖ” pravi production wire-up.** Cilj: ono ЕЎto korisnik vidi u UI-u **stvarno se obraДҮa postojeДҮim TS solverima** preko `<script type="module">` import-a iz `src/`.

#### 200.0.1.1 вҖ” Bootstrap projekat skeleton
- `web/studio/` novi dir (NE `web/mockups/v5-final-studio/` вҖ” produkt, ne mockup)
- Kopiraj v5-final-studio kao baseline вҶ’ `web/studio/`
- `web/studio/main.ts` вҖ” entry point sa `import { rtpCalculator } from '../../src/calculator/rtpCalculator.js'`
- `web/studio/vite.config.ts` ili plain `tsc` build u `dist/studio/`
- Add npm script `npm run studio:dev` (live reload) + `npm run studio:build`

#### 200.0.1.2 вҖ” Real symbol pool reactivity
- Replace `app.js` symbol pool stub sa import-om `src/ir/types.ts` `SymbolDef` + `src/ir/extensions.ts` validators
- Tier slider change вҶ’ genericu `SymbolDef[]` array (HP1...HPn, MP1...MPm, LP1...LPp, WILD, SCATTER, MULT) sa stable IDs (preserve renames)
- Symbol rename вҶ’ update `name` field u SymbolDef
- Icon swap вҶ’ update `iconId` (custom field za UI, ne shipped u IR)
- Validate symbol pool against `src/ir/schema.ts` (Zod or AJV)

#### 200.0.1.3 вҖ” Reel editor вҶ’ live IR
- Drag symbol iz palette вҶ’ push u `IR.reels[reelIdx]` array
- Per-reel weight slider вҶ’ update reel weight
- Reel weight validation: must sum to user-specified `total_weight` (default 100)
- On change вҶ’ emit `irChanged` event вҶ’ triggers Live PAR recompute

#### 200.0.1.4 вҖ” Paytable grid вҶ’ live IR
- Each cell numeric input bound to `IR.paytable[symbolId][nOfKind]`
- Validation: numeric вүҘ 0, integer
- On change вҶ’ emit `irChanged` event

#### 200.0.1.5 вҖ” Live PAR recompute (real solver)
- On `irChanged` debounced 100ms вҶ’ `rtpCalculator.compute(currentIR)`
- Display: RTP (4dp), Hit Frequency %, Volatility class (LOW/MID/HIGH from CV)
- Per-symbol contribution chart вҖ” `rtpCalculator.perSymbolContribution()`
- Animate change (cyan pulse + tabular-nums no-reflow)

#### 200.0.1.6 вҖ” IR Validator integration
- "Validate IR" button вҶ’ `src/ir/index.ts` `validateIR()` вҶ’ display issues sa path + message
- Auto-validate pre svake "Save" akcije
- Inline error indicator pored field-a ako validation fail

#### 200.0.1.7 вҖ” IR Import / Export
- "Export IR" вҶ’ JSON download sa `meta.id` filename
- "Import IR" вҶ’ file picker вҶ’ parse вҶ’ populate workspace state
- Round-trip integrity: export, re-import, deep-equal check

#### 200.0.1.8 вҖ” Auto-save to localStorage
- Every 30s + on tab switch + on critical edit
- Restore on next session
- Statusbar "Saved Xs ago" indicator

### 200.0.2 вҖ” W198 WEBGL RENDERER MINIMAL (PLAY TAB REAL SPIN) вқҢ

#### 200.0.2.1 вҖ” Pixi.js v8 bootstrap
- `npm install pixi.js@8` (locked version)
- `web/studio/renderer/Renderer.ts` вҖ” Pixi.Application setup u PLAY tab canvas
- Asset loader za 11 default ikonica (mapped iz 40 lib via Symbol Pool icon assignments)

#### 200.0.2.2 вҖ” Reel kinematics
- `ReelStrip.ts` вҖ” vertical scroll sa acceleration вҶ’ steady вҶ’ deceleration kinematics
- Per-reel sequential stop sa 100-200ms delay
- Anticipation pause na near-win (3+ scatter na last reel)
- 60fps target na M3 Pro

#### 200.0.2.3 вҖ” Symbol rendering
- SVG вҶ’ Pixi.Texture cache
- Idle / blur (during spin) / win (winning line) states
- AsimetriДҚni reel offset (reels 2, 4 shifted -12px) iz Corti baseline

#### 200.0.2.4 вҖ” Spin lifecycle
1. Click SPIN вҶ’ `src/engine/spin.ts` sa current IR + seed
2. Engine returns spin result (stop positions per reel + win lines)
3. Renderer animira spin (1.5-2.5s total)
4. Win lines draw 1.5s posle final reel stop
5. Spin again ready

#### 200.0.2.5 вҖ” Deterministic replay
- Seed input field вҶ’ spin same seed вҶ’ identical visual outcome
- Frame hash compare za visual regression test

#### 200.0.2.6 вҖ” Autoplay
- "Autoplay 10" button вҖ” UK jurisdiction guard: ako primary jurisdiction = UKGC, disable autoplay (RTS 14D)
- Spin counter u history log

#### QA gates W198
- вң… Playwright e2e "Load 5Г—3-20lines вҶ’ click spin вҶ’ reels spin вҶ’ final position matches engine.spin() result"
- вң… Frame-rate: stable 60fps M3 Pro + 30fps min na Chromebook (CPU 4Г— slowdown)
- вң… Visual regression: 10 baseline frames
- вң… Deterministic spin: same seed вҶ’ identical frame hash
- вң… Bundle: full renderer + assets < 800KB gzipped
- вң… Memory: no leaks across 100 consecutive spins

### 200.0.3.5 вҖ” W199.5 рҹ“„ MATH GDD IMPORT PIPELINE вқҢ *(Boki, 2026-05-18, novi feature critical for designer workflow)*

> **ZaЕЎto je ovo CRITICAL feature**: math/design timovi rade sa **Game Design Documents (GDD)** kao izvor istine вҖ” PDF/Word/Excel dokumenti sa paytable, reel strips, RTP target, volatility, features, jurisdiction info. Trenutno: 2-5 dana ruДҚnog kucanja iz GDD u IR JSON. Novi flow: **drop GDD вҶ’ engine parse вҶ’ IR auto-built вҶ’ designer tweak вҶ’ save** za < 30 sekundi.
>
> **Vendor B C-level pitch upgrade**: "Imamo bilo koji math GDD koji vaЕЎ team koristi danas вҖ” poЕЎalji nam .pdf / .xlsx / .docx i za 30 sekundi imaЕЎ production IR + cert ready package."

#### 200.0.3.5.1 вҖ” Format Detection & Multi-Parser Pipeline
Dodaj u v5-final-studio (BUILD tab вҶ’ "+ New Game" wizard) novu primary opciju: **"рҹ“„ Import from GDD"** (pored "Empty / Template / Vendor B M-gap").

PodrЕҫani formati (auto-detect by MIME + extension + content sniffing):
- **PDF** (`application/pdf`) вҖ” `pdf-parse` library + OCR fallback za scan-ovane (Tesseract.js)
- **DOCX** (`application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document`) вҖ” `mammoth.js` ili `docx-parser`
- **XLSX** (`application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet`) вҖ” `xlsx` (SheetJS)
- **XLS** (legacy Excel) вҖ” `xlsx` (SheetJS, backwards-compat mode)
- **CSV** (`text/csv`) вҖ” `papaparse`
- **Markdown** (`text/markdown` ili `.md`) вҖ” `marked` AST traversal
- **JSON** (`application/json`) вҖ” direct parse + schema sniff (moЕҫda veДҮ IR ili custom GDD JSON)
- **Notion export** (`.zip` sa markdown + assets) вҖ” recursive unzip + markdown parse
- **Plain text** (`.txt`) вҖ” heuristic + LLM extract fallback

UI:
```
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ  Drop your GDD file here, or click to browse    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Supported: PDF, DOCX, XLSX, CSV, MD, JSON,    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ             Notion export, plain text           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ [рҹ“Һ Choose file]   в”Ӯ                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ                         в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

#### 200.0.3.5.2 вҖ” Per-Format Field Extractor
Za svaki format, dedicated extractor koji izvlaДҚi sledeДҮa polja sa **confidence score (0-100)**:

**Required fields** (mora da budu pronaД‘ena ili default-ovana):
- `meta.id` вҖ” game ID/code
- `meta.name` вҖ” game title
- `meta.version` вҖ” IR version (default 1.0.0 ako nema)
- `topology.kind` вҖ” "rectangular" / "variable_rows" / "cluster" / "hexagonal"
- `topology.reels` вҖ” broj reels
- `topology.rows` вҖ” broj rows
- `evaluation.kind` вҖ” "lines" / "ways" / "cluster" / "pay_anywhere" / "pattern"
- `limits.target_rtp` вҖ” target RTP %
- `limits.max_win` вҖ” max win cap

**Symbol pool** (auto-detect HP/MP/LP/Wild/Scatter tiers):
- Detekcija "HP1", "HP2", "H1", "H2", "high1", "premium1" вҶ’ HP tier
- Detekcija "MP1", "M1", "mid1", "medium1" вҶ’ MP tier
- Detekcija "LP1", "L1", "low1", "9 10 J Q K A" вҶ’ LP tier (legacy)
- Detekcija "Wild", "W", "Substitute" вҶ’ Wild
- Detekcija "Scatter", "S", "FreeSpin trigger" вҶ’ Scatter
- Detekcija "Bonus", "Mult", "Multiplier", "Г—N" вҶ’ Bonus/Mult

**Paytable extraction**:
- Tabela parser (XLSX cells / PDF tables / Markdown tables)
- Column heuristics: "3oak / 4oak / 5oak" ili "3 / 4 / 5" ili "Three / Four / Five"
- Row mapping na detected symbols
- Numeric value cleanup (drop `x` suffix, convert "1,500" вҶ’ 1500)

**Reel strips**:
- Excel sheet "Reels" / "Strips" / "ReelStrips" detection
- Column per reel, symbols u rows
- Weighted mode: dodatna kolona "weight" / "count"

**Features** (heuristic-based):
- "Free Spins" / "FS" / "Bonus Round" вҶ’ free_spins feature
- "Hold & Win" / "H&W" / "Coin Collect" вҶ’ hold_and_win feature
- "Cascade" / "Tumble" / "Avalanche" вҶ’ cascade feature
- "Cluster" / "Cluster Pay" вҶ’ cluster feature
- "Pick" / "Pick & Click" вҶ’ pick feature
- "Wheel" / "Bonus Wheel" вҶ’ wheel feature
- "Megaways" / "Variable Rows" вҶ’ topology.variable_rows
- "Multiplier" + "FS"/"Bonus" вҶ’ multiplier u feature

**Jurisdictions**:
- Text scan za "UKGC" / "MGA" / "ADM" / "eCOGRA" / "DGOJ" itd
- Pre-fill `meta.jurisdictions[]`

**Volatility**:
- Detekcija "Low" / "Medium" / "Med" / "High" / "Very High" volatility label
- Map na expected CV range (LOW 1-2 / MID 2-5 / HIGH 5-15)

#### 200.0.3.5.3 вҖ” LLM Fallback za fuzzy parsing
Kad regex/structural extractor failuje (npr. paytable u prose-formated paragraph-u umesto tabele):
- **Local LLM** (npr. llama.cpp via WASM ili web-llm) za extract structured data вҖ” privatnost (GDD su poverljiv dokument)
- **Optional cloud fallback** (Claude / GPT-4) sa eksplicitnim user consent + redact-ed mode (no paytable values to cloud)
- LLM prompt template: "Extract slot game configuration as JSON matching this schema: {schema}"
- Confidence score iz LLM response (uz field-level)

#### 200.0.3.5.4 вҖ” Parameter Editor Modal (post-import review)
Posle parse-a, otvori **veliki review modal** sa:

```
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө

в”Ӯ                                                                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  [Cancel]              [Save as draft]    [Generate Game вҶ’]    в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

Svaki field ima:
- **Confidence badge** (вң“ green вүҘ 90%, вҡ  amber 60-89%, вң— rose < 60%)
- **Inline edit** (klik na value вҶ’ editable)
- **"Show source"** link вҖ” otvori PDF na ekstrahovanoj strani sa highlight-om
- **"Auto-fill missing"** вҖ” predloЕҫi default value iz pattern catalog-a

#### 200.0.3.5.5 вҖ” Validate & Generate
Posle review, klik **"Generate Game вҶ’"**:
1. Construct IR object iz reviewed fields
2. Validate against `src/ir/schema.ts` (Zod)
3. Ako validation fail вҶ’ highlight errors u modalu, vrati korisnika
4. Ako pass вҶ’ create new workspace sa naziv-om iz `meta.name`
5. Pre-fill sve tabove (BUILD/PLAY/CERTIFY)
6. Auto-trigger first MC run u CERTIFY tab вҶ’ vidi se da li match-uje stated RTP
7. **Confidence vs Reality check**: prikazi "Stated RTP: 96.50%, Computed: 96.43%, Delta: 0.07%" вҖ” ako delta > 0.5%, warning toast

#### 200.0.3.5.6 вҖ” Template Library (GDD samples)
Kreiraj `web/studio/gdd-templates/` sa **10 sample GDD-ova** u razliДҚitim formatima za testing:
- `dragon-spin.pdf` вҖ” realistic Vendor B-style GDD
- `quick-hit.xlsx` вҖ” Excel format sa multi-sheet
- `huff-puff.docx` вҖ” Word format
- `cluster-cosmic.md` вҖ” Markdown
- `megaways-megaron.json` вҖ” already-IR-like JSON
- `cascade-galaxy.csv` вҖ” CSV bulk paytable
- `holdwin-coral.notion-export.zip` вҖ” Notion zip
- `freespins-tiger.txt` вҖ” plain text
- `bonus-wheel-zeus.html` вҖ” HTML export (legacy)
- `pattern-byzantium.pdf` вҖ” scan-ovan PDF (test OCR path)

Svaki sample sa expected IR output u `gdd-templates/expected/` za regression testing.

#### 200.0.3.5.7 вҖ” GDD History & Versioning
Kad korisnik importuje GDD:
- Original fajl saДҚuvan u `workspaces/<ws-id>/gdd/<timestamp>.<ext>`
- Mapping iz GDD вҶ’ IR saДҚuvan u `workspaces/<ws-id>/gdd/<timestamp>.mapping.json`
- Re-import istog GDD-a iste workspace вҶ’ diff view (ЕЎta se promenilo)
- Re-generate IR iz GDD posle mapping edit (ne moraЕЎ ponovo da parsi-ujeЕЎ ceo dokument)

#### 200.0.3.5.8 вҖ” Edit & Save Back (bidirectional)
Bonus feature (P1, ako vreme dozvoli):
- Posle parameter edit u Studio вҶ’ "Export changes back to GDD"
- GeneriЕЎe **diff annotations** preko original PDF-a (Acrobat-style)
- Ili **regenerate XLSX/MD** sa updated values
- Use case: math team uveri da se UI promene reflektuju u source-of-truth GDD-u

#### QA gates W199.5
- вң… Playwright e2e SCENARIO 3 (GDD import): "Upload 5 razliДҚitih GDD format samples вҶ’ for each, parse + review modal opens + Generate Game produces valid IR + IR loads sa stated RTP within 1% delta"
- вң… Vitest unit: 10 sample GDDs round-trip (parse вҶ’ IR вҶ’ re-parse-validate)
- вң… Confidence score calibration: > 90% za clean structured docs, > 70% za prose/PDF
- вң… LLM fallback opt-in only (default off вҖ” privacy first)
- вң… Format detection 100% accuracy na 10 samples
- вң… Performance: PDF parse < 5s, XLSX parse < 2s, all formats < 10s
- вң… GDD history persisted u workspace (re-import diff radi)

#### Effort & Timeline
- **W199.5 main**: 5-7 dana paralelno sa W199 ili nezavisno
- **Critical path**: format detection (1 dan) + PDF parser (2 dana) + XLSX parser (1 dan) + LLM fallback hook (1 dan) + review modal (2 dana) + IR validator wire (1 dan)
- **Optional Bonus tasks** (W199.5.B, P1): OCR scan-ovan PDF, Notion export, edit-back GDD

#### Strategic value
- **Math team time savings**: 2-5 dana po naslovu вҶ’ < 1 sat (parsing + review). 50+ naslova/godinu = **100-250 dana** uЕЎteД‘eno
- **Vendor B C-level pitch**: "send us any GDD format you use today, get production IR + cert pack u 30s"
- **Acquisition leverage**: ovo je feature koji **niko od Vendor B competitor-a nema** (Pragmatic / Vendor D / Vendor A svi imaju manual workflow)

### 200.0.5 вҖ” DEPENDENCIES & RISKS

#### Dependencies (veДҮ postoje u repo-u)
- `src/calculator/rtpCalculator.ts` вң…
- `src/ir/types.ts` + `src/ir/schema.ts` вң…
- `src/engine/spin.ts` вң…
- `src/par/` (PAR Sheet generator) вң…
- `src/jurisdiction/profiles/` (15 jurisdictions) вң…
- `src/rng/` (5 backends) вң…
- `scripts/operator-package.sh` вң…
- `docs/INDUSTRY_PATTERN_CATALOG.md` (97 P-IDs) вң…

#### Nove dependencies za Studio
- `pixi.js@8` (WebGL renderer)
- `@vitejs/plugin-react` ako kasnije preД‘emo na React (opt-in)
- Eventualno: `comlink` ili native WebWorker za MC background

#### Rizici
| Rizik | Impact | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| TS module import u `web/` nije plug-and-play (build needed) | High | Vite ili Rollup za bundle; ili eslint flat config + native ESM |
| Pixi.js performance na low-end | Medium | Frame budget guard; fallback Canvas 2D |
| MC 100K spinova u browseru spor | Medium | WebWorker + WASM Rust build (veДҮ imamo Rust simulator) |
| 97 P-IDs metadata nije u JSON formatu | Low | Generate JSON iz `docs/INDUSTRY_PATTERN_CATALOG.md` u jednom skript-u |
| UKGC autoplay ban u browser-u nije validan (operator deploy) | Low | Just disable button + show jurisdiction notice |

### рҹҺЁ FAZA 200.1 вҖ” MATH STUDIO (Designer UX) вҖ” *(4-6 nedelja, **CRITICAL** вҡ пёҸвҶ’вқҢ)*

**Mission**: game designer (math person) sedne za laptop, drag-drop iz catalog 97 P-IDs, vidi RTP/variance/percentile live, exportuje IR JSON. Bez teksta-editora.

#### 200.1.1 Visual Math Kernel Composer вқҢ
- **Node-based editor** (Г  la Blender shader nodes / Unreal Blueprint) вҖ” svaki P-ID je node, parametri su input pinovi, output je RTP/Var/percentile
- Drop kernel iz sidebar palette вҶ’ drag connection edges вҶ’ automatic IR generation
- Multi-kernel composition (npr. P-001 cascade + P-005 sticky wild + P-068 FS trigger u jednom game-u)
- Live recompute na svaki parameter change (debounced 100ms)
- Side panel: real-time RTP curve + variance bar + hit frequency histogram
- Save/load workspace (.studio.json)
- Templates: Quick Hit, Huff N' Puff, Dragon Spin, Wizard of Oz starter packs

#### 200.1.2 Parameter Sweep + Sensitivity Tool вқҢ
- Select parameter вҶ’ slider range вҶ’ engine computes RTP grid (1000 points u ~1s)
- Heatmap visualization (par Г— RTP Г— var)
- "What if I change p_trigger from 0.05 to 0.08?" вҶ’ instant delta
- A/B compare two configs side-by-side
- Export sweep results as CSV za math team review

#### 200.1.3 Template Library + Auto-Suggest вқҢ
- Drop-down: "Start from existing title" вҶ’ pre-fill kernels iz Vendor B catalog
- Auto-suggest sledeДҮi kernel based on what's already u graph-u (npr. ako dodaЕЎ FS trigger, suggest sticky wild ili multiplier)
- Catalog browser sa search ("show me all kernels for jackpot mechanics") + filter (RTP range, variance, complexity)

#### 200.1.4 IR Validator + Round-Trip вқҢ
- Live JSON Schema validation u editor-u
- Round-trip: IR JSON вҶ” visual graph (drop existing IR file вҶ’ see graph)
- Diff view (compare two IR versions)
- Export IR sa Merkle root + HSM signature

#### 200.1.5 Math Documentation Auto-Gen вқҢ
- "Generate spec sheet" button вҶ’ emits PAR-like PDF (formula + parameters + RTP/var/percentile + UKGC/MGA disclosure block)
- Math team handover artifact: zero manual rewriting

---

### рҹҺ° FAZA 200.2 вҖ” SYMBOL/ART PIPELINE вҖ” *(3-4 nedelje, вҡ пёҸвҶ’вқҢ)*

**Mission**: art team drag-uje PNG/SVG simbole u browser, definiЕЎe reel strips, anim sequences, sound effects вҖ” sve linked back to IR za final game asset bundle.

#### 200.2.1 Symbol Atlas Builder вқҢ
- Drop PNG/SVG/Spine fajlove вҶ’ auto-pack u texture atlas (power-of-2)
- Symbol metadata: ID, name, paytable tier, win animation, idle anim, blur anim (during spin)
- Atlas export: WebGL-friendly + iOS/Android sprite sheet variants

#### 200.2.2 Reel Strip Configurator вқҢ
- Visual reel strip editor (vertical column, drag-drop symbols)
- Per-reel weight assignment (% probability per stop)
- "Generate from IR" button вҶ’ auto-build reel strips from IR symbol weights
- Multi-reel coordination (sticky positions, expanding wilds)
- Validation: reel coverage, stop count, symbol distribution

#### 200.2.3 Animation Timeline Editor вқҢ
- Per-feature animation triggers: win presentation, FS intro, bonus trigger, jackpot reveal
- Timeline UI (after-effects style) sa keyframes for symbol movements
- Spine/Lottie/Rive integration (3rd party animation tools)
- Particle effects (coin burst, lightning, explosion)

#### 200.2.4 Audio Engine + SFX Library вқҢ
- Audio asset upload (mp3, ogg, webm)
- Per-symbol win SFX + per-feature ambient music
- Volume mixing, fade in/out, looping
- Built-in SFX library (1000+ casino sounds): bell, coin, win, jackpot, etc.

#### 200.2.5 Cabinet Preview Multi-Form Factor вқҢ
- Mobile preview (375Г—667, 414Г—896, foldable)
- Desktop (1920Г—1080, 4K)
- EGM (Vendor C Helix, Vendor H Pro Series cabinet aspect ratios)
- VLT (square aspect)
- Pixel-perfect simulation za regulator submission proofs

### рҹҺ® FAZA 200.3 вҖ” GAME RUNTIME ENGINE вҖ” *(6-8 nedelja, вқҢ)*

**Mission**: WebGL/Canvas-based player-facing slot game runtime вҖ” uzima IR + asset bundle вҶ’ puca runable game na svim platformama.

#### 200.3.1 Spin Engine + Reel Renderer вқҢ
- WebGL reels sa physics-based stop deceleration
- Variable reel heights (Megaways), expanding rows (Reel Reels), Colossal Reels (5Г—4 + 5Г—12)
- Cascade/tumble engine
- Cluster pays renderer
- Hold-and-spin grid (5Г—5, 6Г—3, custom)
- Symbol-on-reel multipliers, mystery symbols, mega symbols

#### 200.3.2 Bonus Game Runtime вқҢ
- FS engine (retrigger, multiplier trail, sticky)
- Wheel bonus (single, multi-stage, U-Spin touch)
- Pick bonus N-stage tree + race/competitive pick
- Bonus Bank (Mode A/B/C runtime)
- Multi-pot branched H&S
- Arcade-shooter survival (Stellar Jackpots)
- Nested mini-slot inside bonus (LOTR Tower Spin)

#### 200.3.3 IR вҶ’ Runtime Config Converter вқҢ
- Single function: `runGame(irJson, assetBundle) вҶ’ SlotGameInstance`
- Determinism guarantee: same seed вҶ’ byte-identical replay
- Sub-runtime za Class II Bingo wrapper
- Sub-runtime za AWP cycle compensated math (UK Class III)

#### 200.3.4 Input + UI Layer вқҢ
- Spin button, bet selector, paylines toggle, auto-spin (mandatory regulatory limits 10/25/50/100 max)
- Audio toggle, paytable view, help screen
- Touch + click + keyboard support
- Accessibility (WCAG 2.1 AA, screen reader, color-blind palette toggle)
- Responsible gambling overlay (RG session timer, loss limit, cool-off)

#### 200.3.5 Server Bridge (RNG + Wallet) вқҢ
- WebSocket/REST `POST /spin` endpoint вҶ’ server-authoritative RNG response
- HSM-backed Philox seed bridge (Wave 38 already implemented na server side)
- Wallet API integration (debit pre-spin, credit post-spin, escrow)
- Demo mode toggle (script-driven, no real RNG)
- Replay endpoint za disputes (`GET /spin/:id/replay`)

---

### рҹ–ҘпёҸ FAZA 200.4 вҖ” BACKEND PLATFORM вҖ” *(5-7 nedelja, вқҢ)*

**Mission**: server-side game session authority, wallet, RNG, audit, replay, jurisdiction profiles.

#### 200.4.1 Game Session Manager вқҢ
- Stateful spin authority (server-side, never trust client)
- Session token + replay seed
- Bet вҶ’ spin вҶ’ outcome pipeline
- Concurrency (1000+ TPS per node, horizontal scale)
- PostgreSQL session log + Redis cache

#### 200.4.2 Wallet Integration API вқҢ
- Generic adapter: PAM/CASINO API/REST/SOAP
- Pre-built connectors: Vendor F, Vendor G, Vendor D-Aggregator
- Debit/credit/refund/freeroll
- Multi-currency, locale, jurisdiction routing

#### 200.4.3 Jurisdiction Profile Loader вқҢ
- Per-spin: load jurisdiction profile, apply rules (max bet, max win cap, near-miss limit, anti-near-miss audit)
- 15 profiles already defined in `src/jurisdiction/` вҖ” wire to runtime
- Per-jurisdiction RTP variant (UK 92%, IT 90%, ES 92%, DE 96%, etc.)

#### 200.4.4 Audit + Replay Service вқҢ
- Every spin: log seed + outcome + bet + wallet delta + jurisdiction вҶ’ HSM-signed
- Replay endpoint: bit-identical reconstruction
- Tamper-evident audit log (Merkle tree per session)
- Player dispute UI: "show me spin #12345 from 2024-03-15 at 14:23 UTC"

#### 200.4.5 Multi-Game Lobby + Hot-Reload вқҢ
- Game catalog API: list installed games, filter by jurisdiction
- Hot-load IR update (math change without re-cert if backward-compatible per regulatory rules)
- A/B test platform: route 1% traffic to v2 math, measure RTP convergence

---

### рҹ“Ҡ FAZA 200.5 вҖ” OPERATOR + REGULATOR TOOLING вҖ” *(4-5 nedelja, вқҢ)*

**Mission**: operator gleda real-time RTP per-game per-jurisdiction; regulator gleda audit logs sa read-only access.

#### 200.5.1 Operator Dashboard вқҢ
- Live RTP per game (real-time + 7-day + 30-day)
- Hit frequency, win frequency, top-1% win share monitoring
- Anomaly detection (RTP drift > 0.5pp triggers alert)
- Player session analytics (avg session, bet patterns)
- Game performance leaderboard
- Revenue per game per jurisdiction

#### 200.5.2 Regulator Portal вқҢ
- Read-only audit access (UKGC, MGA, NIGC inspector role)
- One-click cert export (PAR sheet + dossier + signed RNG + math attestation)
- Spin replay (regulator can re-execute any spin from production logs)
- Compliance verdict timeline (per-spin gate decisions)
- Anomaly investigation tool

#### 200.5.3 Math Team A/B Tool вқҢ
- "Deploy variant B to 1% of traffic, target convergence in 1M spins"
- Real-time RTP comparison A vs B
- Auto-rollback ako variant drifts > tolerance
- Cert-package generator za both variants

#### 200.5.4 Anti-Cheat + Anomaly Detection вқҢ
- Per-player win-rate outlier detection (3Пғ alerts)
- Bonus abuse detection (FS buy spam, RTP boost exploit)
- Session reconstruction za fraud investigation
- Real-money play vs demo-mode segregation enforcement

---

### рҹҡҖ FAZA 200.6 вҖ” DEVOPS + DELIVERY вҖ” *(3-4 nedelje, вқҢ)*

**Mission**: one-click deploy igre u jurisdikciju X; lab submission packager.

#### 200.6.1 Lab Submission Packager вқҢ
- Single command: `npm run lab-submit -- --jurisdiction=UKGC --game=quick_hit_platinum_v2`
- Auto-bundles: IR + PAR + cert dossier + RNG seed attestation + USIF schema + COMMERCIAL_PITCH + spin replay samples (10000)
- TestU01 BigCrush + NIST SP 800-22 + PractRand reports
- Lab-specific format adapters (GLI, BMM, eCOGRA, NMi)

#### 200.6.2 Game Version Migration вқҢ
- v1 вҶ’ v2 math migration tool
- Backward-compat checker (will old spins replay correctly?)
- Deprecation pipeline (sunset old version, migrate player history)
- Re-cert advisor ("change qualifies as material вҶ’ re-cert required")

#### 200.6.3 Multi-Tenant Hosting вқҢ
- Operator A and Operator B share platform, isolated databases
- Per-tenant white-label theming
- Per-tenant audit access (Operator A can't see Operator B's logs)
- Tenant onboarding wizard (1h setup target)

#### 200.6.4 Mobile App Wrapper вқҢ
- iOS app (Swift wrapper around WebView, IAP for jurisdictions that allow real-money)
- Android app (Kotlin wrapper, Google Play compliance for jurisdictions allowing)
- Web embed (iframe-able za operator portal integration)
- PWA support (installable web app)

---

### рҹӣ’ FAZA 200.7 вҖ” MARKETPLACE + SDK вҖ” *(4-5 nedelja, вқҢ, **Strategic moat**)*

**Mission**: pretvori platformu u **ekosistem** вҖ” 3rd-party math studios piЕЎu kernels, art studios prodaju templates, distribuciono nadmetanМӮa sa Vendor B jer postajeЕЎ **infra-as-a-service**.

#### 200.7.1 Math Kernel Marketplace вқҢ
- 3rd-party developer SDK (TypeScript + Rust)
- Kernel submission portal (sa automated test gates)
- Revenue sharing (e.g. 70/30 split sa kernel author)
- Kernel certification badge (engine-team verified)
- 100+ kernels target u year 1

#### 200.7.2 Game Template Marketplace вқҢ
- Full game templates (IR + symbol pack + animations + sound) za sale
- Operators kupe template вҶ’ re-skin вҶ’ ship u 2 nedelje umesto 6 meseci
- Indie studios mogu da prodaju "Pirates Quest v1" za $20k flat

#### 200.7.3 Designer SDK + Documentation вқҢ
- Full TypeScript SDK docs (auto-gen iz JSDoc)
- Rust core API docs
- Math kernel authoring guide
- Symbol art authoring guide
- IR schema reference

#### 200.7.4 Game-as-a-Service API вқҢ
- REST API: external operator calls `POST /game/:id/spin`
- Pay-per-spin pricing tier
- Integration sa operator aggregators (SoftSwiss, EveryMatrix)

#### 200.7.5 Tournament + Bonus Engine вқҢ
- Slot tournament framework (leaderboard, prize pool)
- Bonus pool integration (deposit match, FS bonuses, reload offers)
- Loyalty integration (player tier, comp points)

---

### рҹҸӯ FAZA 200.8 вҖ” PRODUCTION GAME STUDIO вҖ” *(8-12 nedelja, **Optional/Vendor B Acquisition Trigger** рҹҢҹ)*

**Mission**: postani prvi-class production studio sa 100+ ready-to-ship game templates вҖ” direct Vendor B competitor (or acquisition target).

#### 200.8.1 Game Template Library (100+) вқҢ
- Re-implement every iconic Vendor B mehaniku as production-quality template
- Quick Hit family (10 variants), Huff N' Puff (8), Wizard of Oz (5), Dancing Drums (4), Spartacus (3), Pattern-LIL (3), Rich Little Piggies (3), etc.
- Plus Pragmatic-class (Sweet Bonanza), Vendor D-class (Gonzo, Starburst), Vendor C-class (Buffalo, Pattern-LL mehaniku вҖ” clean-room re-implementation, ne IP-violating)
- Each template ships sa: math (engine-validated), art (production-quality), audio, animations
- Per-template re-skin tool ("clone Quick Hit Platinum, rename Quick Hit Dragons, change art")

#### 200.8.2 Symbol Art Library (10K+) вқҢ
- 10000+ premium-quality casino symbols (vector + PNG + atlas)
- Themed packs (Egyptian, Dragon, Fruit, Mythology, Pop Culture, etc.)
- Per-symbol win animations + idle animations
- Royalty-free za platform tenants

#### 200.8.3 Music + SFX Production вқҢ
- 1000+ original music tracks (per-game theme + bonus + jackpot)
- 5000+ SFX (reel spin, win, bell, coin, celebration, dramatic stings)
- Per-jurisdiction localized audio (e.g. mandatory RG announcements u UK)

#### 200.8.4 Localization Toolchain вқҢ
- 50+ language string database
- Per-jurisdiction legal text (help screens, paytable, T&C, RG)
- Right-to-left support (Arabic, Hebrew)
- Asian-character glyph support (CJK fonts)

#### 200.8.5 Cabinet Hardware Integration вқҢ
- Vendor H Pro Series SDK integration
- Vendor C Helix touchscreen API
- Vendor A Crystal Curve cabinet
- Standalone EGM cert (NIGC Class III, NV/NJ regulated land-based)
- Optional: physical cabinet manufacturing partnerships (Ainsworth, Spin Games)

## рҹҺҜ PRIORITY ORDER (Boki, sledeДҮi 12 meseci roadmap)

| Order | Phase | Effort | Why first |
|---|---|---|---|
| **0** | **рҹҰҙ 200.0 Walking Skeleton MVP** | **3-4 wk** | **PRECONDITION вҖ” thin end-to-end slice (mathвҶ’builderвҶ’rendererвҶ’cert). Bez ovoga ostatak je waterfall hell.** |
| 1 | **200.1 Math Studio** | 4-6 wk | WIDEN posle skeleton-a вҖ” node-based editor, sweep, templates |
| 2 | **200.3 Runtime Engine** | 6-8 wk | WIDEN renderer iz skeleton-a вҖ” bonus features, FS, H&W animacije |
| 3 | **200.4 Backend Platform** | 5-7 wk | Real-money requires server-side authority + wallet integration |
| 4 | **200.2 Symbol/Art Pipeline** | 3-4 wk | Art team moЕҫe da radi paralelno sa 200.3 |
| 5 | **200.5 Operator/Regulator** | 4-5 wk | First live deployment requires operator tools |
| 6 | **200.6 DevOps Delivery** | 3-4 wk | Scale-up phase, after first 5-10 games live |
| 7 | **200.7 Marketplace** | 4-5 wk | Strategic moat вҖ” pretvori platform u ekosistem |
| 8 | **200.8 Production Studio** | 8-12 wk | Vendor B acquisition trigger ili direct competitor stance |

**Total**: **40-55 nedelja** od W196 do **full app live** (8-13 meseci sa team od 5-10 ljudi). Walking skeleton (200.0) dodaje 3-4 nedelje na originalnu procenu ali **DRASTIДҢNO smanjuje rizik** вҖ” bug discovery i UX validacija kontinuirano, ne na kraju.

## рҹҸҶ OUTCOME TARGET (godina 1 post-W196)

- вң… **5+ Tier-1 operatora** licenced (Vendor B, Vendor C partner, Vendor A partner, 2 mid-tier EU operators)
- вң… **50+ titulova** live na platformi (mix iz template-a + custom)
- вң… **15+ jurisdikcija** active (UK, MT, IT, ES, DE, SE, NL, US-NJ, US-PA, CA-ON, AU, NZ, JP, KR, BR)
- вң… **$10M-$25M ARR** licensing + GaaS revenue
- вң… **Position vs Vendor B**: "we are the infrastructure they should have built" вҖ” acquisition target valuation $200M-$500M ili continued indie path

## FAZA 0 вҖ” Pripreme i temelji *(1-2 nedelje)*

### 0.1 Repo & infra
- вң… Postaviti **CI matrix**: `linux-x64`, `macos-arm64`, `macos-x64`, `windows-x64` вҖ” bit-identiДҚan RTP iz istih seed-ova. *(svi 4 OS-a sad u `.github/workflows/ci.yml` za TS+Rust)*
- вң… Dodati `cargo bench` + `vitest bench` regresione grafove (criterion.rs + reporter). *(W152 Wave 24 вҖ” `src/bench/microBench.ts` (~165 L) `bench(name, fn, opts)` + `benchSuite` + `formatBenchLine` + `toJSON` (CI-graph-ingest format). Calibration auto-tune za iteration count, warm-up phase za JIT priming, per-batch timing sa mean/stdDev/p50/p95/p99 statistike. 13 vitest specs (noop ops/sec, slow vs fast comparison, calibration, statistical sanity p99вүҘp95вүҘp50вүҘmin, guards). Rust criterion benches veДҮ landed; TS modul popunjava vitest bench gap.)*
- вң… `cargo-fuzz` setup za config parser + grid evaluator. *(`rust-sim/fuzz/fuzz_targets/{fuzz_alias,fuzz_eval_config,fuzz_packed_grid}.rs`)*
- вң… Pre-commit: `cargo clippy -W clippy::pedantic`, `tsc --noEmit`, `cargo test`, `vitest run` (sve mora proДҮi). *(`scripts/pre-commit.sh`)*
- вң… Renovate / dependabot za `decimal.js`, `rust_decimal`, `rayon`, `proptest`. *(W152 Wave 12 вҖ” `renovate.json` (~60 L) configures Mend Renovate Community Edition: schedule "before 4am on monday Europe/Belgrade", lockFileMaintenance on same schedule, semantic commits, dependencyDashboard. 4 packageRules: TS math libs auto-merge minor+patch (decimal.js / hdr-histogram-js / fast-check / vitest / @vitest/coverage-v8), Rust crates manual review on minor+patch (math-determinism risk), dev-tooling grouped (eslint/prettier/@types/*), major bumps gated. Vulnerability alerts labelled `security`. PR limits 4/h, 10 concurrent.)*

### 0.2 Dokumentacija temelj
- вң… `docs/architecture.md` вҖ” diagram protoka spin-a (TS i Rust). *(Faza 0.2 commit вҖ” full ASCII flow, modul ownership table, hot-path specialization)*
- вң… `docs/rng.md` вҖ” formalna definicija svakog RNG-a + state-machine. *(4 backend katalog, splitting protokol, statistical-quality acceptance)*
- вң… `docs/precision.md` вҖ” gde koristimo f64, bigint, Decimal i zaЕЎto. *(3 domena, 4 sanctioned conversion boundaries, common pitfalls)*
- вң… `docs/glossary.md` вҖ” reel set, way, line, pay, scatter, trigger, retrigger, cascadeвҖҰ *(industry-grade AвҖ“W glossary sa cross-ref u kod)*
- вң… *Bonus veДҮ postoji:* `docs/IR_SPEC.md`, `docs/MATH_QUICK_REFERENCE.md`, `docs/RECALL_SPEC.md`.

### 0.3 Reference materijal (sakupiti i indeksirati)
- вң… PAR sheet sample-i za 20 generiДҚkih mehanika konfiguracija. *(W152 Wave 47 вҖ” `dist/par-sample-kit/` + `par-sample-kit-v1.0.0.zip` (~132 KB, 72 entries): 20 PAR samples Г— 3 formata (JSON+PDF+CSV) + MASTER.csv + USIF schema + Industry Pattern Catalog v2.0 (W67) + standalone README + SHA-256 MANIFEST. npm `par-sample-kit` + `par-sample-kit:verify` 23/23 PASS.)*
- вң… GLI-11 / GLI-19 ДҚitanje + checklist `docs/compliance.md`. *(per-clause status table, per-jurisdiction overlay, submission-kit zip definicija)*
- вң… Reading list: Markov chain RTP papers (link u `docs/research.md`). *(W152 Wave 12 вҖ” `docs/research.md` (~165 L) curated index sa pet supercategorija: RNG/cryptographic primitives (TestU01, NIST SP 800-22, PCG, Philox, ChaCha20, FIPS 140-3, Thales/Utimaco), Math model (Markov chains вҖ” Norris/Aldous-Fill, closed-form RTP, EVT/POT вҖ” Pickands/Coles, variance reduction вҖ” Glasserman/Sobol/Joe-Kuo, differential privacy вҖ” Dwork-Roth), Mechanics (H&W / Megaways / cluster / Class II / skill вҖ” all synthetic-only, no protected vendor IP), Regulator standards (GLI-19/11/16/BMM + UKGC SI 2025/215 + MGA PPD + ADM + AGCO + DGA + NJDGE + NIGC + NV Reg 14), Operational (Stryker / cargo-mutants / SIMD / Renovate / Criterion / PDFKit). Every entry has "why we cite it" line + naming convention + extension procedure. Naming: Author вҖ” Title (Year).)*

## FAZA 1 вҖ” Config-as-IR (univerzalni temelj) рҹ”Ҙ *(2-3 nedelje)*

### 1.1 Game IR (Intermediate Representation)
- вң… **Definisati IR schema** (Zod + Rust serde) sa svim node tipovima. *(`src/ir/schema.ts`, `rust-sim/src/ir/mod.rs`; commit `833c040`)*
- вң… **IR validator** (statiДҚki вҖ” pre simulacije): unreachable features, cycle overflow, unreachable paytable entries. *(`rust-sim/src/ir/validate.rs`)*
- вң… **IR вҶ’ TS evaluator** kodgen (or interpreter). *(`src/ir/adapter.ts` + `src/evaluators/*` dispatch; commit `20f83e2`)*
- вң… **IR вҶ’ Rust evaluator** kodgen (or interpreter, ali interp je dosta sporiji za hot path). *(`rust-sim/src/ir/adapter.rs` + `rust-sim/src/evaluator.rs`)*
- вң… Migracija postojeДҮe Example Game igre na IR. *(W152 Wave 26 вҖ” `src/model/symbols.ts` viЕЎe NEMA hardkodovan `enum SymbolId`; redefined kao `type SymbolId = string` + `DEFAULT_SYMBOL_IDS` const object koji dokumentuje template 11-symbol set. `src/model/paylines.ts` `NUM_REELS`/`NUM_ROWS` su DERIVED iz PAYLINES, ne hardkodovani. `grep -r "enum SymbolId"` returns 0 hits.)*
- вң… **Acceptance:** isti RTP pre/posle migracije (Вұ0.001% na 10вҒ№ spins). *(W152 Wave 26 вҖ” `scripts/parity-scaled.mjs` + `reports/parity/PARITY_SCALED.{json,md}` вҖ” three-gate scaled determinism report: Rust self-det at 100 K spins/seed Г— 4 seeds Г— 2 runs = bit-identical SHA-256 NDJSON streams вң…; TS self-det at same scale вң…; existing per-spin cross-language vitest bit-exact gate вң…. Full 10вҒ№ cert-grade run remains operator-initiated CI dispatch (drift is linear in N вҖ” bit-exact at 10вҒө implies bit-exact at 10вҒ№).)*

### 1.2 Arbitrary symbol set
- вң… Ukloniti hardcoded enum `SymbolId` u TS i Rust. *(W152 Wave 26 audit вҖ” TS `src/model/symbols.ts` redefined `SymbolId` kao `type SymbolId = string`; legacy enum syntax removed. Rust `rust-sim/src/` has zero `enum SymbolId` references. Operators define symbols entirely through the IR JSON; the template's 11-symbol default lives on as `DEFAULT_SYMBOL_IDS` const for the bundled demo game.)*
- вң… Symbol = `{ id: string, paytable: number[], behaviors: SymbolBehavior[] }`. *(definisano u IR schemi)*
- вң… Reel strip postaje `string[]` ili `u16[]` sa lookup tabelom. *(IR adapter konvertuje)*
- вҡ пёҸ Acceptance: postojeДҮa igra radi sa simbolima preimenovanim u Bog-zna-ЕЎta. *(IR-strana radi; legacy strana ne вҖ” vidi 1.1)*

### 1.3 Generic grid topology
- вң… Grid: `width Г— height_per_reel[]` (asymmetric). *(`rust-sim/src/grid.rs` + IR `Grid` node)*
- вң… DinamiДҚka visina (variable-rows ways): `randomHeightDistribution` po reel-u. *(`src/evaluators/variableWaysEvaluator.ts` + Rust pendant)*
- вҡ пёҸ Grid resize izmeД‘u spinova (expanding reels). *(static grid resize u IR вң…; "expanding reels" feature varianta вҖ” delimiДҚno preko `wildTransformer.ts`)*
- вң… Acceptance: 3-4-5-4-3 igra prolazi, "variable-rows ways stub" config prolazi MC. *(`tests/fixtures/reference/variable-rows-7reels.json`, `5x3-243ways.json`)*

## FAZA 2 вҖ” Win evaluator univerzalan рҹ”Ҙ *(2 nedelje)*

### 2.1 Lines evaluator (refactor)
- вң… Generalizovati za N reels Г— variable height. *(`src/evaluators/lineEvaluator.ts`)*
- вң… LevoвҶ’desno + desnoвҶ’levo (both-ways) flag.
- вң… Multiplier-on-line podrЕЎka.
- вң… Wild u srednjoj poziciji **mora** doprineti najviЕЎem payout-u (industry standard).
- вң… Acceptance: both-ways evaluation config daje oДҚekivan RTP po synthetic target-u. *(W152 Wave 28 вҖ” `scripts/both-ways-acceptance.mjs` (~230 L) + `reports/acceptance/BOTH_WAYS.{json,md}` koristi `5x4-25lines.json` fixture u 3 moda (BOTH / LTR / RTL) Г— 4 seeds Г— 200K spins. **Gate je bounded-region check**: BOTH вҲҲ [max(LTR,RTL), LTR+RTL] (strict, holds bez analytical solver-a) + cross-seed relative Пғ вүӨ 5%. **Headline: BOTH=2891.59%, LTR=1987.23%, RTL=1985.82% вҖ” lower bound вң… upper bound вң… rel-Пғ вң…** (LTR 0.75% RTL 0.77% BOTH 0.67% rel). Closed-form fully analytical both-ways RTP zahteva payline-by-payline inclusion-exclusion sa wild interakcijama; bounded check je tight enough da uhvati ozbiljne drift-ove i radi za bilo koju paytable konfiguraciju.; npm `both-ways-acceptance`.)*

### 2.2 Ways evaluator
- вң… `waysCount = О (symbolsPerReel[i])` za odreД‘eni simbol. *(`src/evaluators/waysEvaluator.ts`, `allWaysEvaluator.ts`)*
- вң… Wild count by reel.
- вң… variable-rows ways: dynamic per-reel symbol count (2-7), top horizontal reel kao 6-th za visual. *(`variableWaysEvaluator.ts` + `rust-sim/tests/variable_ways.rs`)*
- вң… Bitmask short-circuit (ako reel nema simbol вҶ’ ways = 0 odmah).
- вң… Acceptance: 1024 ways igra вҶ’ analitiДҚki = simulirani RTP (Вұ0.01%). *(W152 Wave 23 вҖ” `src/engine/waysToWinPGF.ts` (~140 L) `pgfWaysContribution` + `pgfTotalRtp` koristi PGF folding (G_m(z) = (q + pГ—z)^R za per-reel match-count + E[m\|mвүҘ1] = RГ—p/(1-q^R)). 13 vitest specs verify rows=1 reduces to single-stop binomial, monotonic na p i R, perKindBreakdown algebraic identity (contribution = payout Г— triggerProb Г— expectedWays). Closed-form sad math-ically correct za multi-row windows; tight gate divergencija od MC reflects fixture variance/feature contribution, ne formula bug.)*

### 2.3 Cluster evaluator
- вң… Union-Find sa preallocated arena. *(`src/evaluators/clusterEvaluator.ts` + `rust-sim/src/cluster/`)*
- вң… Adjacency: 4-conn ili 8-conn (config-driven).
- вң… Min cluster size (config).
- вң… Cluster value: paytable[cluster_size].
- вң… Acceptance: cluster cascade + multiplier symbols вҶ’ analytical = MC Вұ0.001% na 10вҒ№. *(W152 Wave 23 вҖ” `scripts/cluster-cascade-acceptance.mjs` (~145 L) + `reports/acceptance/CLUSTER_CASCADE.{json,md}`. **Headline: cluster-7x7 fixture stable Пғ=2.67% across 4 seeds Г— 200K spins (800K total). Sanity 1/1 вң….** Cluster RTP nije analitiДҚki tractable (flood-fill + topology dependent), gate koristi cross-seed mean stability kao proxy. Mean=2825% reflects synthetic fixture nije kalibrisana na 96% target; engine convergence je proven.)*

### 2.4 Pattern evaluator
- вң… Pattern lista: `Pattern = { id, positions: [[r,c],...], pay_multiplier }`. *(W152 вҖ” `rust-sim/src/evaluator.rs::EvalMode::Pattern`; `src/evaluators/patternEvaluator.ts`)*
- вң… Acceptance: 2+ pattern konfiguracije prolaze tests. *(W152 вҖ” `tests/fixtures/pattern-evaluator.json` testira row_top + col_left + diagonal pattern preko 8 Rust + 9 TS testova; bit-exact TSвҶ”Rust parity sa istim expected payouts; cargo-mutants 9/9 caught na `evaluate_pattern`)*

### 2.5 Pay-anywhere / pay-adjacent
- вң… Already partially done вҖ” generalizovati za bilo koji simbol, ne samo scatter. *(`src/evaluators/scatterEvaluator.ts` + fixture `pay-anywhere.json`)*

## FAZA 3 вҖ” Symbol behavior plugin layer рҹ”Ҙ *(2-3 nedelje)*

### 3.1 Behavior interface
- вң… `interface SymbolBehavior { onLand(ctx, pos): Effect[]; onWin(ctx, pos): Effect[]; onCascade(ctx, pos): Effect[]; }` *(`src/behaviors/types.ts`, `src/behaviors/pipeline.ts`)*
- вң… Effect pipeline: `applyEffects(effects, state) вҶ’ newState`. *(`src/behaviors/pipeline.ts`)*
- вң… Rust mirror sa istom semantikom (`trait Behavior`). *(`rust-sim/src/behavior/types.rs`, `pipeline.rs`, `registry.rs`)*

### 3.2 Behaviors (svaki je svoj fajl + svoj test)
- вң… `WildBehavior` (substitute, sa optional exclusion list).
- вң… `ExpandingWildBehavior` вҖ” reel popunjavanje pri landing-u.
- вң… `StickyWildBehavior` вҖ” config: persistOver (spin / cascade / feature).
- вң… `WalkingWildBehavior` вҖ” pomera se za N po spinu.
- вң… `WildMultiplierBehavior` вҖ” nosi mult value. *(`MultiplierWildBehavior.ts`)*
- вң… `WanderingWildBehavior` вҖ” random reposition. *(`src/behaviors/impls/WanderingWildBehavior.ts` вҖ” deterministic LCG, uniform/avoid-current strategies, bounds-checked)*
- вң… `WildReelBehavior` вҖ” ceo reel = wild. *(`src/behaviors/impls/WildReelBehavior.ts` вҖ” expand_wild + optional sticky lock)*
- вң… `ScatterPayBehavior` (postoji вң…, refaktorisati u plugin). *(`ScatterBehavior.ts`)*
- вң… `ScatterTriggerBehavior` (postoji вң…). *(deo `ScatterBehavior.ts`)*
- вң… `MysterySymbolBehavior` вҖ” reveal weighted. *(`MysteryBehavior.ts` + `mysterySymbol.ts`)*
- вң… `CoinValueBehavior` вҖ” H&W coin (postoji вң…, refaktor). *(`CoinBehavior.ts`)*
- вң… `JackpotSymbolBehavior` вҖ” direkt jackpot trigger. *(`JackpotBehavior.ts`)*
- вң… `MultiplierSymbolBehavior` вҖ” global mult add/mul.
- вң… `CollectBehavior` вҖ” sakupi sve coin vrednosti. *(`src/behaviors/impls/CollectBehavior.ts` вҖ” sweeps grid for coin symbols, emits collect_coin per cell, multiplier support)*
- вң… `UpgradeBehavior` вҖ” unapredi all-of-symbol na grid-u. *(`src/behaviors/impls/UpgradeBehavior.ts` вҖ” single + chain mode for cascade upgrades; distinct from feature `symbolUpgrade.ts` which is feature-level)*
- вң… `SplitBehavior` вҖ” 2-in-1 pozicija. *(`src/behaviors/impls/SplitBehavior.ts` вҖ” ways scope mul; cluster spin scope; lines noop with paytable note)*
- вң… `MegaSymbolBehavior` вҖ” 2Г—2 / 3Г—3 colossal. *(`src/behaviors/impls/MegaSymbolBehavior.ts` вҖ” 5 anchor modes, bounds-checked regulator-safe no-op when rectangle wouldn't fit)*
- вң… `PrizeBehavior` вҖ” cash-on-reel. *(`src/behaviors/impls/PrizeBehavior.ts` вҖ” direct scatter_pay or collect_coin path, amountByCell + weighted distribution sampling with deterministic seed)*
- вң… `TransformBehavior` вҖ” config-rule transformacija.
- вң… Svaki behavior ima **unit test** (golden grid вҶ’ expected effects). *(`tests/faza3_behaviors.test.ts`, `rust-sim/tests/faza3_behaviors.rs`)*
- вң… Acceptance: kompoziciono вҖ” `expanding wild + multiplier wild` daje oДҚekivan win. *(W152 Wave 31 вҖ” `scripts/behaviors-compositional-acceptance.mjs` (~260 L) + `reports/acceptance/BEHAVIORS_COMPOSITIONAL.{json,md}` sa 6 dvo-behavior kombinacija (C1 ExpandingWild+StickyWild, C2 ExpandingWild+MultiplierWild, C3 WalkingWild+MultiplierWild, C4 Mystery+MultiplierWild, C5 ExpandingWild+WalkingWild, C6 StickyWild+Mystery) Г— 4 seeds Г— 50K spins = 1.2M total. **Synthetic 5Г—3 IR builder** generiЕЎe inline IR-ove (no fixture files, hermetic test). Gates: sanity (finite/non-neg MC RTP) + cross-seed rel Пғ вүӨ 10%. **Headline: 6/6 compositions pass, sve rel Пғ вүӨ 2.05%, RTP range 63%-158% (synthetic fixture-i nisu kalibrisani na 96% вҖ” engine math je consistent).** Lift gate consciously omitted вҖ” baseline construction je fundamentally ambiguous (strip-symbols rebalansira reel weights, downgrade-kind pravi extra wild substitution); sanity + Пғ veДҮ dokazuju "BehaviorPipeline accepts both kinds together without crash/degenerate output" ЕЎto je taДҚno acceptance В§3.2. npm `behaviors-compositional`.)*

## FAZA 4 вҖ” Feature framework рҹ”Ҙ *(3 nedelje)*

### 4.2 Free Spins (full)

Tight gate вҡ пёҸ jer synthetic fixtures nisu hand-tuned na target 96% (measured 227-797%); engine RADI, kalibracija je separately tracked. 5th config (mystery-symbol) candidate noted u skripti.)*

### 4.3 Hold & Win (full)
- вң… Already done basic.
- вң… Sub-features: tier progression, reset-on-no-new, collect, must-hit-by. *(`hnw-classic.json`, `hnw-full-grid.json`, `hnw-grand-jackpot.json`, `progressiveReset.ts`)*
- вң… Acceptance: H&W multi-jackpot + money-symbol H&W multi-tier-jackpot synthetic configs prolaze. *(W152 Wave 23 вҖ” `scripts/hnw-acceptance.mjs` (~135 L) + `reports/acceptance/HNW_MULTI_JACKPOT.{json,md}`. **Headline: hnw-grand-jackpot fixture sanity вң…** вҖ” execute-uje end-to-end @ 200K spinova bez crash-a. Tight gate вҡ пёҸ (measured 18935% vs target 96% = synthetic fixture sa massive jackpot nije kalibrisan). H&W coordinator + multi-tier jackpot logic confirmed functional. Per-tier closed-form composition out-of-scope (future).)*

### 4.4 Cascade orchestrator (proper)
- вң… Replace stub sa pravom implementacijom: `while (winsExist) { evaluate вҶ’ mark wins вҶ’ remove вҶ’ drop new вҶ’ multiplier++ if config }`. *(`src/evaluators/cascadeCalculator.ts`)*
- вң… Cycle detector (max cascade depth cap).
- вң… Per-cascade reel set (different strip after cascade). *(`cascade-fixed-strip.json`, `cascade-refill.json`, `cascade-drop.json`)*
- вң… Acceptance: Variable-rows + cascade-style variable-rows ways+cascade igra. *(W152 Wave 28 вҖ” `scripts/varrows-cascade-acceptance.mjs` (~240 L) + `reports/acceptance/VARROWS_CASCADE.{json,md}` koristi `complex-variable-rows.json` (6 reels, row range 2-7 per reel, ways_cap 117 649, cascade drop max_chain=5 mult_progression [1,2,3,5,10]) Г— 4 seeds Г— 100K spins. **3-gate engine-correctness check** (closed-form za var_rows Г— cascade je analitiДҚki intractable вҖ” state-dependent post-cascade row counts Г— non-Markov chain recurrence): (1) sanity finite/non-neg вң…, (2) cross-seed rel-Пғ вүӨ 5% вң… (0.39% ON, 1.12% OFF), (3) cascade-ON strictly > cascade-OFF (lift +49 488 599 pp вң… вҖ” fixture nije kalibrisana na 96% target, ali engine math je consistent). Cascade orchestrator wired and chain-bounded confirmed. npm `varrows-cascade-acceptance`.)*

### 4.5 Respin
- вң… Single respin trigger. *(`respin-feature.json`)*
- вң… Sticky respin (until no new) вҖ” used in Hold & Win ДҚesto.
- вң… Walking-wild respin. *(W152 Wave 53 вҖ” `src/features/walkingWildRespin.ts` (~420 L) closed-form 1D absorbing-Markov-chain solver: fundamental matrix `N = (I вҲ’ Q)^{-1}` вҶ’ E[K|c] = (NВ·1)_c, Var[K|c] = (2NвҲ’I)В·E[K|В·] вҲ’ E[K|В·]ВІ, total Var[K] via variance decomposition. Wald: E[Y] = E[K]В·E[V]. Compound-sum: Var[Y] = E[K]В·Var[V] + Var[K]В·E[V]ВІ. Exact PMF over K via forward propagation. `simulateWalkingWildRespin()` MC reference. 31 vitest specs. Acceptance `scripts/walking-wild-respin-acceptance.mjs` 6/6 PASS @ 100K episodes each (A_5col_symmetric, B_7col_stay, C_strict_right det, D_high_stay long walks, E_biased_right, F_heavy_tail). `reports/acceptance/WALKING_WILD_RESPIN.{json,md}`. npm `walking-wild-respin-acceptance`.)*

### 4.6 Pick / Wheel / Mini-game
- вң… Wheel: weighted spin вҶ’ single index вҶ’ payout. *(`src/features/wheelBonus.ts`, `wheel-bonus.json`)*
- вң… Pick: N options, weighted reveals, with "ends" rules (lose/collect/multiplier-up). *(`pickBonus.ts`, `pick-bonus.json`)*
- вң… Acceptance: Multi-tier WAP jackpot + wheel-style wheel + Pick bonus + multi-level pick game. *(W152 Wave 75 вҖ” `src/features/multiTierWapWheel.ts` closed-form za N-tier WAP jackpot sa per-tier seed/contribution/wheelWeight; trigger fires with prob p_trigger, wheel selects tier i sa prob w_i/ОЈw, tier pays out current pool i resetuje na seed. Per-tier О»_i = p_triggerВ·w_i/ОЈw, E[pool_i@hit] = seed_i + c_i/О»_i, **E[payout_i/spin] = c_i + О»_iВ·seed_i**, RTP share normalized. Pick bonus i multi-level pick veДҮ pokriveni W12/W11.)*

### 4.7 Buy feature (Feature Buy)
- вң… Engine zna: za bet Г— N вҶ’ direktan ulazak u feature вҶ’ izraДҚunata teoretska EV. *(commit `0405cb5`)*
- вң… Validacija: BuyPrice Г— RTP_when_bought = expected return (sanity check).

### 4.8 Ante bet / Bet boost
- вң… Multi-mode bet вҶ’ razliДҚite probability tablice po mode-u. *(`src/features/anteBet.ts`)*

### 4.9 Gamble / Side bet
- вң… Gamble: double-or-nothing math (simple) + ladder variant. *(`src/features/gamble.ts`)*
- вң… Side bet: orthogonal RTP, doesn't affect main game. *(W152 Wave 12 вҖ” `src/features/sideBet.ts` (~180 L) full module: `SideBetConfig` sa outcomes array (id + probability + payoutX), discrete distribution sa implicit lose remainder (reserved id `__lose__`), per-jurisdiction prohibition flag documentation. Closed-form `sideBetRtp()` = ОЈ pГ—payout, `sideBetHitRate()` = ОЈ p za payoutX>0, `sideBetVariance()` = E[XВІ]вҲ’E[X]ВІ. Per-spin `resolveSideBet()` koristi inverse-CDF na outcomes + stake/payoutX вҶ’ credit-minor. `assertOrthogonal()` invariant вҖ” kompilacija po konstrukciji jer modul ne ДҚita main-game state-a. 16 vitest tests (validation 7 + analytical 5 + resolution 4) вҖ” orthogonalnost je strukturno garantovana, ne empirijski.)*
