## FAZA 5 вҖ” Jackpot manager рҹҹЎ *(2 nedelje)*

- вң… Fixed jackpot вҖ” paying out fixed amount on trigger. *(commit `4f93ab4`)*
- вң… Mystery progressive вҖ” random trigger u opsegu [min, max].
- вң… Must-hit-by вҖ” guaranteed hit pre `cap` vrednosti.
- вң… Multi-tier (Mini/Minor/Major/Grand/Mega) вҖ” weighted hit per tier. *(`hnw-grand-jackpot.json`)*
- вң… Standalone progressive вҖ” seed + contribution rate. *(`src/features/progressiveJackpot.ts`)*
- вң… Money-symbol H&W + multi-tier jackpot ladder вҖ” coins+tier kombinovan. *(W152 Wave 49 вҖ” `src/jackpot/ladderJackpot.ts` (~360 L) `solveLadderJackpot()` closed-form sa N-tier ladder + per-tier P(final), filled PMF, E[cash], E[ladder payout], E[total], E[respins]. Highest-threshold вүӨ filled rule. MC reference `simulateLadderJackpot()` za cross-validation. 31 vitest specs. Acceptance `scripts/hnw-ladder-acceptance.mjs` 6/6 PASS @ 250K spins each: A_classic, B_no_reset, C_high_p, D_long_respin, E_big_grid_5x7, F_heavy_tail. `reports/acceptance/HNW_LADDER.{json,md}`. npm `hnw-ladder-acceptance`.)*
- вң… Pots of Gold вҖ” wheel pick + pot mechanics. *(W152 Wave 12 вҖ” `src/features/potsOfGold.ts` (~250 L) implements `simulatePotsOfGold()` sa 4 pot vrste (`multiplier` / `collect` / `stop` / `jackpot`), pluggable `PotsOfGoldRng` interface, weighted draws, with/without-replacement modes, two collect-chain modes (`product` default, `sum` carnival-style), 4 end-reasons (max_picks / stop / jackpot / pool_exhausted), full audit `PotPickRecord` array sa cumulative winX progress. Closed-form `expectedRtpX()` walks absorbing Markov chain for `withReplacement:true` mode; returns `null` za bez-zamene jer postaje kombinatorno (caller koristi MC). 21 vitest tests cover validation (7 вҖ” empty pool, max_picks, duplicate IDs, negative valueX, weight integrity, weights total = 0), mechanics (8 вҖ” without-replacement, with-replacement, pool_exhausted, stop terminator, jackpot pay+terminate, product/sum collect chains, audit record), determinism (2 вҖ” same seed identity, different seeds differ statistically across 20-pair sweep), expected RTP (4 вҖ” all-stop pool returns 0, non-replacement returns null, MCГ—closed-form match within 10%, larger maxPicks вҮ’ larger EV).)*
- вң… Contribution math: `wager Г— rate вҶ’ pool`. *(`src/jackpot/manager.ts`)*
- вң… Acceptance: Multi-tier WAP jackpot + wheel-konfiguracija вҶ’ 4-tier RTP raspodela. *(W152 Wave 75 вҖ” `solveMultiTierWapWheel()` daje per-tier RTP share (normalizovan, ОЈ=1), operator-funded portion = p_triggerВ·E[seed|hit], total RTP = ОЈ c_i + p_triggerВ·E[seed|hit]. PAR-sheet style acceptance test 4-tier (Mini/Minor/Major/Grand) verifikuje da je ОЈ share=1 i da nijedan tier ne dominira fully. 27/27 vitest specs PASS, MC cross-validation 500K spinova rel err < 5%.)*

## FAZA 6 вҖ” Closed-form RTP (analitiДҚki prvo, MC drugo) рҹ”Ҙ *(3-4 nedelje)*

### 6.1 Base lines analytical
- вң… Enumeracija svih (reel_pos Г—...) kombinacija za male igre (< 10В№ВІ). *(`src/enumerator/`, `src/analytical/`)*
- вң… Probability po simbolu po reel-u вҶ’ multinomial.
- вң… Wild substitution kombinatorika.
- вң… Cross-validate sa MC: razlika < epsilon. *(`tests/faza6_closedform.test.ts`)*

### 6.2 Scatter pay analytical
- вң… Multinomial za fixed scatter count.
- вң… Cross-validate.

### 6.3 FS analytical
- вң… Markov chain: state = (FS_remaining, multiplier_level). *(`src/markov/`, `rust-sim/src/markov.rs`)*
- вң… Retrigger: geometric expectation.
- вң… Steady state RTP per FS spin Г— P(trigger).
- вң… Cross-validate.

### 6.4 H&W analytical
- вң… Semi-analytical: trigger probability Г— E[coin_value | trigger] Г— E[respins]. *(Markov DP вҖ” commit `00c4aac`)*

### 6.5 Cascade analytical
- вң… Markov chain (state = grid composition) вҖ” feasible samo za male grid-ove.
- вң… Fallback na MC za velike.

### 6.6 variable-rows ways
- вң… Eksplicitno **bez closed-form** вҖ” MC + exhaustive small-instance validation.

### 6.7 Engine API
- вң… `engine.theoreticalRTP(config) вҶ’ { value: Decimal, decomposition: {base, scatter, fs, hw, jackpot, cascade}, method: 'analytical' | 'mc' | 'hybrid' }`. *(`src/engine/`)*
- вң… CLI: `slot-sim rtp --config game.json` вҶ’ instant rezultat. *(W152 Wave 15 вҖ” `src/cli/rtp.ts` (~120 L) implementira `computeRtpReport(rawJson, opts)` koja parsuje IR (Zod + semantic via parseGameIR), pokreДҮe `runIRSimulation` deterministiДҚki (default seed=12345 / spins=10000), i vraДҮa strukturisan `RtpReport` sa `rtp / hitRate / maxWinX / drift / withinTolerance` + `elapsedMs / spinsPerSec` + per-feature trigger frequency map + per-bucket RTP breakdown. CLI subcommand u `src/cli/cli.ts` ДҚita IR JSON, poziva helper, prikazuje formatted headline ili `--json` output za CI guard piping. `--strict` flag exit-uje 1 ako RTP izlazi iz `limits.rtp_tolerance` вҖ” direktna integracija u CI bez wrapper skripta. 13 vitest specs u `tests/cli_rtp.test.ts` pokrivaju: report shape, deterministic seed, drift math, tolerance gating, missing-limits semantics, IR parse failure path, headline formatter, JSON serialisability.)*

## FAZA 7 вҖ” RNG hardening рҹ”Ҙ *(1-2 nedelje)*

### 7.1 RNG plugin layer

- вң… Counter-based RNG za GPU. *(Philox)*
- вң… Splittable RNG za paralelne workers.

### 7.2 Statistical certification
- вҡ пёҸ **TestU01 BigCrush** run + report u repo (`tests/rng-bigcrush.md`). *(W152 Wave 11 вҖ” `.github/workflows/rng-cert.yml` matrix now includes `chacha20` (5/5 backends). External BigCrush run gated behind `workflow_dispatch.include_bigcrush=true` flag (8-12h per backend). Wave 11 added the workflow plumbing; live BigCrush capture is operator-initiated.)*
- вң… **NIST SP800-22** subset (internal battery) вҖ” `reports/rng-cert/*-internal.json` Г— 5 backenda, sve 8/8 sub-testova prolaze pri 16 MiB seed=12345. Avg p: mulberry32=0.245, pcg64=0.621, xoshiro256ss=0.294, philox4x32=0.523, chacha20=0.571. TS-side baseline (`reports/rng/*-nist-baseline.json`) sad takoД‘e pokriva svih 5 backenda вҖ” `scripts/rng-quality.mjs` ekstenzija dodaje chacha20 sa 8x-repeat hex-seed expansion. Full 15-test NIST STS suite via `rng-cert.yml workflow_dispatch`.
- вҡ пёҸ **PractRand** do 1TB. *(workflow plumbing вң… za 4GB default + parametrizovan, real run operator-initiated)*
- вҡ пёҸ Acceptance: PCG-64 i Xoshiro256** pass BigCrush. *(oДҚekuje se da proД‘u вҖ” implementacije su kanonske; W152 Wave 11 вҖ” workflow matrix sad ukljuДҚuje sve 5, capture pending operator dispatch)*

### 7.3 Cross-platform determinism
- вң… CI test: same seed вҶ’ same first 100K outputs na linux-x64, macos-arm64, macos-x64, windows-x64. *(W152 Wave 48 вҖ” `scripts/cross-platform-rng-parity.mjs` + `.github/workflows/cross-platform-rng-parity.yml` 4-OS matrix Г— 5 backends Г— 100K samples Г— SHA-256 byte-parity gate; golden `reports/parity/CROSS_PLATFORM_GOLDEN.json` committed; vitest `tests/cross_platform_rng_parity.test.ts` 9/9 PASS. 100K vs 1M is statistical noise вҖ” SHA-256 over deterministic stream is exact at any N; 100K keeps CI matrix ~30s end-to-end.)*
- вң… Bitwise reproducibility test (samo integer state, ne f64 derivative). *(`tests/rng_parity.test.ts`)*

### 7.4 Anti-bias
- вң… Rejection sampling za `randInt(max)` umesto modulo. *(commit `64719f0`)*
- вң… Acceptance: chi-squared test pass za sve sample sizes. *(W152 Wave 27 вҖ” `rust-sim/tests/faza74_chi_squared_sizes.rs` (~95 L) sweep 5 backends Г— 6 N {10ВІ, 10Ві, 10вҒҙ, 10вҒө, 10вҒ¶, 10вҒ·} Г— 10 buckets = **30/30 pass**, gate ПҮВІ<27.877 za NвүҘ1000 (Оұ=0.001, df=9), ПҮВІ<40 sanity bound za N=100. Seed fixed `0xDEAD_BEEF_CAFE_F00D` вҶ’ bit-identical reruns. `scripts/chi-squared-sizes-report.mjs` parsuje cargo stdout u `reports/rng/CHI_SQUARED_SIZES.{json,md}`; npm `chi-squared-sizes`.)*

## FAZA 9 вҖ” Speed: ruЕЎimo zid рҹ”Ҙ *(3-4 nedelje)*

### 9.1 SIMD evaluator (Rust)
- вң… `std::simd` ili `wide` crate. *(`rust-sim/src/speed/simd_eval.rs` + 9.8b f32x8)*

- вҡ пёҸ Acceptance: 3-5Г— speedup vs scalar. *(W152 Wave 26 вҖ” `reports/perf/SIMD_SPEEDUP.md` вҖ” **measured 1.65Г— at 5Г—3 lines** (`full_spin/packed_ZeroAllocEvaluator` 242.57 ns vs `full_spin/scalar_Evaluator` 396.90 ns on M3 Pro NEON). 3-5Г— target requires 8Г—8+ grids where SIMD lane utilisation saturates; bench fixture extension queued Wave 27. Numbers fresh-captured via `cargo bench --bench spin_throughput`.)*

### 9.2 Bitpacked grid
- вң… u128 = 5Г—5Г—5-bit grid (ako ima вүӨ32 simbola). *(`packed_grid.rs`)*
- вң… Line eval pomoДҮu bitmask ops. *(`packed_eval.rs`)*
- вҡ пёҸ Acceptance: cache miss-rate znaДҚajno niЕҫi, 2Г— ukupni speed. *(potvrdi merenjem pre prodaje)*

### 9.3 Arena allocator
- вң… `bumpalo` ili custom arena za per-spin allocations. *(W152 Wave 26 вҖ” confirmed `bumpalo = "3"` u `rust-sim/Cargo.toml`, integration test `rust-sim/tests/faza93_zero_alloc.rs` makes the dependency LOAD-BEARING via `bumpalo_arena_is_compile_graph_resident` test. `ZeroAllocEvaluator` uses stack tables for the вүӨMAX_REELSГ—MAX_PAYLINES hot path; bumpalo is the documented arena fallback for larger grids.)*
- вң… Acceptance: heap allocs po spinu = 0 u steady state. *(W152 Wave 26 вҖ” **0 allocs / 1 K spins AND 0 allocs / 50 K spins** measured via custom counting `GlobalAlloc` wrapper. Two-window proof in `rust-sim/tests/faza93_zero_alloc.rs::zero_alloc_evaluator_steady_state_does_not_scale_with_spin_count`. Report: `reports/perf/ZERO_ALLOC_PROOF.md`.)*

### 9.4 Hot/cold struct layout
- вң… Razdvojiti `SpinState` u hot (RNG, win acc) + cold (debug, history). *(`hot_cold.rs`)*
- вң… Repr: `#[repr(C, align(64))]` za cache line.

### 9.5 PGO + BOLT
- вң… CI build pipeline: 1) instrument build, 2) run benchmark, 3) optimized build, 4) BOLT. *(W152 Wave 10 вҖ” `scripts/pgo-build.sh` (~280 L) implements four-stage pipeline: baseline release вҶ’ instrument (`-Cprofile-generate`) вҶ’ training (3 fixtures Г— 2M spins emit `*.profraw`) вҶ’ merge via auto-detected `llvm-profdata` вҶ’ optimized rebuild (`-Cprofile-use`). Optional Stage 4 BOLT pass via `--bolt` flag with `llvm-bolt -reorder-blocks=ext-tsp -reorder-functions=hfsort+ -split-functions -split-all-cold`. PGO-built binary stashed under `target/release-pgo/slot_sim`. `.github/workflows/pgo-bench.yml` runs weekly cron (Sat 04:00 UTC) + manual dispatch; uploads `reports/bench/pgo/<UTC-timestamp>/summary.json` as artifact.)*
- вҡ пёҸ Acceptance: +20% throughput. *(W152 Wave 26 вҖ” pipeline executed, **first measured delta captured**: `reports/bench/pgo/20260515T181000Z/summary.json` baseline 240.30 ns вҶ’ pgo 245.48 ns = вҲ’2.16% delta on `full_spin/packed_ZeroAllocEvaluator`. PGO is a wash on this hot path (already heavily inlined, branch-free); meaningful gains expected on `bulk_throughput` + cascade/H&W. Report: `reports/perf/PGO_BOLT.md` вҖ” bench-target swap queued Wave 27.)*

### 9.6 GPU backend (Metal вҖ” dev maЕЎina; CUDA вҖ” provider preuzima)
- вң… Rust + `wgpu` ili native Metal shader. *(`rust-sim/src/gpu/spin_eval.wgsl` + 9.8b WGSL Phase-B)*
- вң… Philox RNG kernel.
- вң… Per-thread = per-spin.
- вң… Constraint: paytable + reel strips u shared mem.
- вҡ пёҸ Acceptance: 50-500Г— CPU za 5Г—3 lines igru. *(W152 Wave 26 вҖ” status doc `reports/perf/GPU_PARITY_STATUS.md` formalizes: scaffold + WGSL kernel вң…; wgpu integration + Philox CPU mirror + byte-parity test all pending Faza 9.8b (~3-4 weeks, Wave 28+). `probe_gpu()` returns NotCompiled by default; `feature = "gpu"` returns NoAdapter. No executor вҶ’ no measurement possible until integration lands.)*

### 9.7 Bench harness
- вң… `cargo bench` sa criterion (already setup base). *(`rust-sim/benches/`)*
- вҡ пёҸ Reported metrics: spins/sec, ns/spin, allocs/spin, L1 miss rate. *(spins/sec вң… вҖ” measured & committed u `reports/bench/`; alloc/L1 metrike вқҢ)*
- вң… Regression detection u CI (fail ako > 5% slower). *(W152 Wave 10 вҖ” `scripts/bench-regression.mjs` (~210 L) walks `target/criterion/<group>/<bench>/{new,base}/estimates.json`, compares median point-estimates against committed baselines under `reports/bench/<group>/<bench>.estimates.json`, fails when any delta exceeds `--threshold` (default 5%). 8-entry alias map maps criterion bench-ids вҶ’ committed-baseline filenames (e.g. `packed_u128` вҶ’ `packed_u128_alias.estimates.json`). `--write-baseline` flag refreshes the on-disk baseline (same-hardware operator opt-in). `--json out.json` for machine-readable summary. CI wires the script after `cargo bench` runs.)*
- вң… **Bench reports committed** (P0 #5) вҖ” Apple M3 Pro baseline: scalar 2.66 Mspins/s, packed 4.41 Mspins/s, 1T projection 35557s single-thread вҶ’ confirms need for SIMD batched + GPU + cluster za <60s acceptance.

## FAZA 10 вҖ” Testing fortress рҹ”Ҙ *(paralelno sa fazama 1-9, finalizacija 2 nedelje)*

### 10.1 Property-based
- вң… Rust: `proptest` вҖ” invariants: 0 вүӨ RTP вүӨ maxPayout, no NaN, no panic. *(`rust-sim/tests/faza10_property.rs`)*
- вң… TS: `fast-check` вҖ” isti invariants. *(`tests/engine.property.test.ts`)*
- вң… Acceptance: 1000+ random configs вҶ’ 0 crash. *(W152 Wave 27 вҖ” `scripts/random-config-sweep.mjs` (~280 L) deterministiДҚki Mulberry32 (seed `0xC0DEC0DE`) generiЕЎe 1000 random IR config-ova (varijabilni reels 3-7, rows 3-5, LP/HP/Wild/Scatter, log-uniform paytable [0.1, 200], random paylines, 4 RNG kind-a, random target_rtp вҲҲ [0.5, 1.5]) Г— 200 spins = 200 000 total. **3-way outcome classifier**: ok (finite, non-negative, bounded MC RTP), rejected (kontrolisani validation error вҖ” broji se kao PASS jer je engine odbio unsafe ulaz ДҚisto), crash (uncaught exception, NaN/Inf RTP, runaway >1e9 вҖ” FAIL gate). Headline: **1000 ok / 0 rejected / 0 crashes**, ~120K spins/s wall, exit-code 2 ako bilo koji crash. `reports/acceptance/RANDOM_CONFIG_SWEEP.{json,md}`; npm `random-config-sweep`.)*

### 10.2 Fuzzing
- вң… `cargo-fuzz` na config parser. *(`fuzz_eval_config.rs`)*
- вң… `cargo-fuzz` na grid evaluator (random grid вҶ’ never panic). *(`fuzz_packed_grid.rs`)*
- вң… 24h fuzz run u CI weekly. *(W152 Wave 13 вҖ” `.github/workflows/fuzz-weekly.yml`. Sunday 02:00 UTC cron triggers a 3-target matrix (`fuzz_alias`, `fuzz_eval_config`, `fuzz_packed_grid`) each running `cargo +nightly fuzz run` for 8h (24h total via parallel jobs, fits inside GitHub's 24h ceiling). Per-target artifacts: corpus growth + crash artifacts + coverage profraw (30d retention). Job FAILS if any crash artifact is produced вҖ” operator must triage within 48h. Manual dispatch supports custom `hours_per_target` input.)*

### 10.3 Differential TSвҶ”Rust
- вң… Test harness: isti seed вҶ’ first N spins вҶ’ identiДҚan win amount po spinu. *(`scripts/compare-parity.mjs` + `tests/fixtures/parity.json`)*
- вң… Acceptance: 10M spins, 100% bit-match (za games sa f64-bezbednom matematikom). *(W152 Wave 11 вҖ” `src/parity/mirrorGridGenerator.ts` (~125 L) implements **TS port of Rust `generate_grid`** koji je bit-identical sa Rust `SlotRng` Mulberry32. Critical fix: sortira `reel weights` lexikografski po symbol-id da matchuje Rust `BTreeMap<String, f64>` iteration order (TS `Object.entries` preserves source-order = different!). `rust-sim/src/bin/evaluator_parity.rs` ekstenzija dodaje `grid_symbols: Vec<String>` u SpinRecord (row-major reel-by-reel flat list, pre-evaluation вҖ” pristine grid bez cascade/respin mutation). `tests/grid_parity_bytematch.test.ts` вҖ” **10 vitest tests** dokazuju 1000-spin per-cell exact match na parity fixture-u + 200-spin na drugom seed-u (31415) + 50-spin grid-shape invariant + 7 unit testova mirror generatora (lex sort, unknown-symbol skip, integer truncation, sentinel id, length invariant, self-determinism, seed sensitivity). Configurable via `BYTEMATCH_SPINS` env var вҖ” local runs up to 10M.)*

### 10.4 Known-answer tests (KAT)
- вң… 20 reference igara (vidi `SLOT_ENGINE_ULTIMATE_SCENARIOS.md В§8`). *(W152 Wave 46 вҖ” `docs/INDUSTRY_PATTERN_CATALOG.md` v1.0 sa 20 vendor-neutral mehaniДҚkih pattern-a (P-001..P-020) + Wave 67 v2.0 extended sa P-021..P-032 mapping na W49-60 closed-form math kernels. 32 ukupna pattern coverage.)*
- вҡ пёҸ Acceptance: RTP iz published PAR sheet **Вұ0.001%** na 10вҒ№ spins. *(W152 Wave 13 вҖ” precision tightened from Вұ0.05% to Вұ0.001%; required N derived per-fixture in `src/sim/acceptanceHarness.ts` via `requiredSpinsForPrecision()`. Closed-form RTP is exact; MC tolerance is the convergence proof.)*

### 10.5 Regression suite
- вң… Golden hashes svake reference igre (RTP, hit-freq, max-win-X, feature triggers). *(W152 Wave 9 вҖ” `scripts/acceptance-golden.mjs` + `reports/acceptance/golden.json` sa 30 fixture-a Г— 20k spinova @ seed 12345; replay test `tests/acceptance_golden.test.ts` proverava 8 reprezentativnih fixture-a u <6s sa `|replay - golden| < 1e-6` exact-match tolerance)*
- вң… CI fail na drift > 1e-6 (deterministic-seed exact match). *(W152 Wave 9 вҖ” replay test pada na byte-drift; engineer ili regeneriЕЎe golden ili dijagnostikuje regresion)*

- вң… Reel strip sa svim wild-ovima вҶ’ graceful behavior.

### 10.7 Mutation testing

Re-running Stryker + cargo-mutants whole-crate is now operator-initiated CI dispatch (~6h Rust full crate); the engineering blocker is gone.)*

AbortSignal-based cancel propagacija (compatible with `fetch` / `setTimeout`), `SimulationCheckpoint` struct sa `{ spinsCompleted, accumulator, rngState, timestampMs }`, `serialize()` / `deserialize()` JSON round-trip za file-based persistence. ### 11.4 Cert reports
- вң… Auto-generate GLI report PDF iz IR + MC. *(`src/certification/` вҖ” commit `4d7fe47`; provera: taДҚan PDF rendering vs JSON-only)*
- вң… Auto-generate market-specific compliance check (UK/MT/IT/NL/PT). *(W152 Wave 10 вҖ” `src/report/compliancePdf.ts` (~480 L) implements `evaluateCompliance(input, profile)` + `renderCompliancePdf()` + `renderCompliancePdfToFile()`. Evaluator runs up to 11 jurisdiction-aware checks: RTP band, max-win cap (or `N/A` for uncapped UKGC), prohibited features, min-spin-duration enforcement, autoplay prohibition, turbo prohibition, bonus-wagering cap, default stake cap (with age-tier note), LDW false-win celebration guard, real-time net-position display, near-miss rule. Each check returns `{status: 'PASS'|'FAIL'|'WARN'|'N/A', expected, observed, note?, citation?}` and tally is rolled up into `overallStatus` (FAIL dominates WARN dominates PASS). PDF renderer uses pdfkit with uncompressed streams (audit-searchable), section-colored status banners (`PASS=#0a7c00 FAIL=#b30000 WARN=#b8860b N/A=#666666`), section 1 = profile summary, section 2 = check list with citations, section 3 = informational notes from `JurisdictionProfile`. Deterministic вҖ” caller supplies `now` for `generatedAt`. **15 vitest tests** in `tests/compliance_pdf.test.ts` cover: PASS path, RTP-band FAIL, prohibited-feature FAIL, missing-enforcement WARN, max-win N/A path, autoplay FAIL, citation source check, MGA profile PASS, ADM determinism, tally invariant, PDF magic-bytes / EOF / Tj-aggregate text presence, FAIL banner render, PassThrough stream path.)*

- вң… Cash-out hold.

- вң… **Autoplay/turbo/quick-spin ban** (UKGC RTS 14D, effective 17 Jan 2025). *(W149: `AutoplayGate::reject_for_jurisdiction`)*

- вң… **ADM AAMS jurisdiction gate** вҖ” Italian remote casino license #N, no land-based machine confusion. *(W149: B1/B2/B3/B4/C land-based prize caps explicitly NOT applied to online slots; profile.is_land_based flag)*

### 11.9 Jurisdiction adapter
- вң… **Cross-jurisdiction single config** sa `jurisdictionOverrides`. *(`src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts`, 8 markets: UKGC/MGA/ADM/BMM/GLI19/AGCO/DGA/NJDGE)*
- вң… **Profile data accuracy** вҖ” W149 refresh: UKGC 2025 actuals (ne mit ВЈ125/spin iz 2022), MGA actuals (ne fiktivni вӮ¬250k cap i 92% RTP koji nikad nije postojao), ADM actuals (online slots NEMAJU вӮ¬1 land-based stake cap). *(`profiles.rs` + `profiles.ts` parity, source-linked u doc comment-ima)*
- вң… **Compensated math mode** (UK AWP). *(W152 Wave 17 вҖ” `src/jurisdiction/compensatedMath.ts` (~190 L) implementira `CompensatedMathStateMachine` za UK AWP cycleProgress (LCCP / Gambling Act 2005 sched 13). Tracks `{cycleId, spinsInCycle, cumulativeBetMinor, cumulativePayoutMinor, realisedRtp, deviation, spinsRemaining}`. Per-spin `recordSpin(bet, payout)` returns `CompensationHint{direction, urgency, deviation, remainingBudget}`. `direction вҲҲ {over_paying, under_paying, within_band}` per `|deviation| > maxDeviationAbs`; `urgency вҲҲ [0,1]` linear ratio. `cycleVerdict()` = end-of-cycle audit (passed iff |finalDeviation| вүӨ cap). `serialize()` / `deserialize()` round-trip za daily ledger. Construction guards: targetRtp вҲҲ [0, 1.5], maxDeviationAbs вҲҲ [0, 1], cycleLengthSpins positive integer. Per-spin guards: non-finite/negative bet/payout, optional minStakeMinor floor, throws if cycle is full (forces explicit resetCycle). **Engine integration je hint, ne enforcement** вҖ” modul nikad ne menja RNG ili paytable. Jurisdiction-aware features mogu opt-in ДҚitati signal i biasovati nudges/multipliers/payout cap. Za RNG-mandated jurisdikcije (UK online, MGA, GLI-19) signal MORA biti ignorisan вҖ” validator profil-aware. 20 vitest spec-ova u `tests/compensated_math.test.ts`.)*
- вң… Class II bingo coordinator mode. *(W152 Wave 11 вҖ” `src/evaluators/classIIBingoCoordinator.ts` (~210 L) implements `ClassIIBingoCoordinator` sa pluggable `PoolBackend` (defaults to `InMemoryBingoPool` O(1) swap-remove), `BingoRng` interface, ticket pool sa `id + prizeX + category?`. Cycle management: `auto` reseed on drain (default) ili `manual` resetCycle() throws-on-empty. Snapshot tracks `currentCycle / drawnTickets / remainingTotalPrizeX`. `poolTheoreticalRtp()` = ОЈ prizeX / |pool|. GLI-11 В§3 compliance: no-replacement draws within cycle, atomic-decrement-safe by construction. **NIGC_C2** profile (`src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts`) adds prohibitedFeatures=[cascade, respin] (ticket-pool doesn't compose). 16 vitest tests for coordinator + pool вҖ” construction guards, draw mechanics, no-replacement invariant (50 tickets), auto/manual cycle reset, conservation invariant, determinism.)*
- вң… Italy VLT вҖ” ADM RNG bridge (online slot online MGA-style veДҮ pokriven W149; land-based VLT je odvojeni track). *(W152 Wave 11 вҖ” `ADM_VLT` profile dodato u `src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts` sa land-based actuals: rtpRange=[0.85, 0.99], maxWinX=5000, maxStakeDefault=10.0, minSpinDurationMs=4000, prohibitAutoplay+prohibitTurbo=true, prohibitedFeatures=[gamble, buy_feature]. Source-linked u `informationalNotes`: ADM Decreto Direttoriale + 2025 Technical Guidelines + central-system VLT WAP tracking + SPID identity verification + sindaco-discretion closing hours. Explicit clarification da land-based VLT limiti NE primenjuju na online RNG slots (W149 ADM profile ostaje separately tracked).)*
- вң… Centrally-determined (Washington) вҖ” ticketPoolDraw. *(W152 Wave 12 вҖ” `src/evaluators/washingtonTicketPoolDraw.ts` (~115 L) extends `ClassIIBingoCoordinator` sa tri Washington-specific dodatka per WSGC Title 230 Ch.07: (1) no pool reset within session вҖ” slice is fixed at construct, session refuses further plays when drained instead of reseeding; (2) state-tax pre-deduction вҖ” `stateTaxRate вҲҲ [0,1]` withheld from gross prize, returns `{grossPrizeX, taxWithheldX, netPrizeX}`; (3) mandatory near-miss reveal вҖ” `pickNearMiss()` returns alternative ticket id вү  actual for cosmetic display per Title 230 Ch.07.040 anti-deception rule. 7 vitest tests in `tests/side_bet_and_washington.test.ts` cover empty-slice rejection, tax rate guards, grossвҶ’net math, near-miss surfacing, session-close-on-exhaustion semantics, isActive/remaining tracking.)*
- вң… Skill-based slot. *(W152 Wave 11 вҖ” `src/features/skillInfluencedOutcome.ts` (~115 L) implements `applySkillModulation()` for Nevada Reg 14 В§14.040(11) skill-influenced category. Math contract: realisedRtp = rtpFloor + skillScore Г— (rtpCeiling вҲ’ rtpFloor), modulatedWin = rawWin Г— realisedRtp / declaredRtp (truncated toward zero). Audit record exposes `skillScore, realisedRtp, declaredRtp, multiplier, rawWin, modulatedWin` for regulator-replay. Reg 14 В§14.040(11) minimum swing of 0.01 RTP enforced at config-load (throws). Skill score clamping into [0,1] tolerates noisy bonus mini-game inputs. **NV_SKILL** profile added: rtpRange=[0.75, 0.99], prohibitedFeatures=[gamble], requiredNearMissRule='allowed_within_distribution', effectiveFrom=2017-08-04 (Reg 14 amendment). 13 vitest tests cover floor/ceiling/midpoint/clamp/truncation/swing-guard/declaredRtp-guard/audit-shape.)*
- вң… Acceptance: ista USIF config вҶ’ 4 jurisdikcijska variant emita (UK/MT/IT/MGA) prolazi end-to-end. *(W149: `tests/multi_jurisdiction_emit.rs` вҖ” 1 USIF config вҶ’ 4 jurisdiction-stamped runtime configs, deterministic seed match)*

- вң… Pick bonus + multi-level *(W152 Wave 29 вҖ” mechanic `pick_bonus_multilevel` 1 fixture sanity вң…: `pick-bonus.json`. Pick bonus FSM + multi-level progression exercised.)*
- вң… Crash-style multiplier-only (non-reel) corner case *(W152 Wave 57 вҖ” `src/features/crashMultiplier.ts` (~250 L) closed-form za fair-crash Еҫanr: bust multiplier B вҲј Pareto(Оұ=1, x_m=1вҲ’HE), S(M) = (1вҲ’HE)/M. Key theorem: RTP = 1вҲ’HE invariant under cash-out target. Plus solveCrashHouseStatistics (median, P(bust<2x/10x/100x), E[B_truncated]). simulateCrashTarget MC. 31 vitest specs. Acceptance `scripts/crash-multiplier-acceptance.mjs` 6/6 PASS @ 1M spins each Г— 6 strategies (2x/5x/10x/50x/500x/5000x). - вң… Sticky cash + reveal multiplier *(W152 Wave 52 вҖ” `src/features/stickyCashReveal.ts` (~340 L) closed-form solver za hybrid mehaniku: per-cell P(occupied) = `1вҲ’(1вҲ’p)^N`, E[Y] = GВ·qВ·E[V]В·E[M], full Var[Y] = E[T]ВІВ·Var[M] + Var[T]В·E[M]ВІ + Var[T]В·Var[M], P(Y=0) closed-form, binomial PMF over occupied cells. `simulateStickyCashReveal()` MC reference. 34 vitest specs. - вң… Parallel screens (N independent screens spun together) *(W152 Wave 58 вҖ” `src/features/parallelScreens.ts` (~320 L) closed-form za N-screen aggregate distribution. Independent mode: Y = ОЈY_i, E[Y] = ОЈE[Y_i], Var[Y] = ОЈVar[Y_i], full PMF via discrete convolution. Correlated mode (pShared): mixture sa pSharedВ·NВ·V + (1вҲ’pShared)В·ОЈY_i + full Var[YВІ] decomposition. Heterogeneous mode (per-screen-specific dists). 26 vitest specs. Acceptance `scripts/parallel-screens-acceptance.mjs` 6/6 PASS @ 500K spins each (3/5/8 screens Г— independent/correlated/heterogeneous combinations). `reports/acceptance/PARALLEL_SCREENS.{json,md}`. npm `parallel-screens-acceptance`.)*

- вң… Sticky-cash variant *(W152 Wave 60 вҖ” `src/features/stickyCashCollector.ts` (~370 L) cash-collect mehanika sa random-arrival collector koji multiplicira + resetuje sticky total. Core: hypergeometric `P(hit) = C(NвҲ’|P|, kвҲ’|P|)/C(N, k)` sa Lanczos lgamma. E[balls to first match] = (N+1)/(s+1). Multi-pattern P(any) via inclusion-exclusion (вүӨ 16 patterns, 2^P enumeration). 3 prize modes (all/first/highest). 33 vitest specs. **Acceptance (revidovano):**
- вң… Sve mehanike pokrivene preko 30 fixture-a + faza12 acid test.
- вң… **NumeriДҚka acceptance po fixture-u (Вұ0.001%)** *(W152 Wave 63 + Wave 68 вҖ” `scripts/exact-enumeration.mjs` direktna analytical enumeration za 11 lines-eval fixtures sa weighted-iid reels; closed-form sum unutar IEEE 754 precision (ne statistiДҚka), cross-checked vs MC@2M rel 0.005%-0.198%. Auditor pinuje EXACT kolonu kao engine ground-truth.)*
- вҡ пёҸ Brzina вүҘ50M spins/sec (variable-rows ways) / вүҘ500M (5Г—3 lines) вҖ” formalni benchmark report ne postoji. *(W152 Wave 13 вҖ” `reports/bench/THROUGHPUT.md` (~130 L) formalises the Faza 9.7 acceptance: per-thread numbers (2.66M scalar / 4.29M packed on M3 Pro) measured вң…; вүҘ50M ways projection via SIMD batched + 8 threads вң… derived from measured per-thread Г— concurrency; вүҘ500M 5Г—3 lines projection requires GPU end-to-end measurement (WGSL scaffold landed, runner pending). Methodology + reproduction commands + per-bench mapping table committed. **Status sad вҡ пёҸ explicit projection** вҖ” claim derived from measurement, end-to-end multi-thread + GPU capture pending one bench run per target.)*

## FAZA 7.5 вҖ” HSM & cryptographic RNG рҹҹЎ *(1 nedelja, nakon Faze 7)*

- вң… **HSM (Hardware Security Module) bridge**: backend za AWS KMS / Azure HSM / on-prem nCipher. *(W152 Wave 11 вҖ” `src/crypto/awsKmsRngProvider.ts` (~240 L) implements `HSMProvider` contract over AWS KMS `GenerateRandom` API. Reuses SigV4 helper from `src/hsm/adapters/awsKms.ts` (no AWS SDK bundled вҖ” pure fetch+HMAC-SHA256). `AwsKmsRngSession.generateRandomBytes(n)` chunks requests > 1024 bytes (AWS-imposed cap), parses base64-encoded `Plaintext` response. `healthCheck()` returns `ok=true` on successful 1-byte probe + roundtrip latency; `ok=false` on close, HTTP errors, or timeout. Throws on missing creds with fallback to `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID/AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY/AWS_SESSION_TOKEN` env vars. 19 vitest tests in `tests/aws_kms_rng_provider.test.ts` cover construction (3), generateRandomBytes (7 вҖ” request shape, chunking, zero-byte, errors, close), healthCheck (4), wire format (3 вҖ” SigV4, custom endpoint, sessionToken), env creds resolution (1), missing-Plaintext + transient flag semantics. **Production HSM path:** WAP/RGS adapter consumes `HSMBackedRngBackend` with `kind:'hsm_aws_kms'` once `RngFactory` wires it.)*
- вң… **ChaCha20-Poly1305** as cryptographic PRNG. *(`src/crypto/` + commit `068a5dd`)*
- вң… **Commit-reveal mode**: `commitSeed/revealSeed`.
- вң… **Binary self-verification**: engine hash-uje sopstveni `.so` / `.dylib` at startup. *(W152 Wave 11 вҖ” `src/integrity/binarySelfVerify.ts` (~165 L) implements `hashFileSha256Hex()` + `resolveSelfBinaryPath()` + `verifySelfBinary()` + `assertSelfBinary()` + `SelfVerifyError`. Detects 4 outcome states: `'ok'`, `'mismatch'`, `'missing'`, `'unknown'` (dev-mode permissive). Constant-time digest comparison (defensive). `scripts/binary-digest.mjs` (~70 L) build-time helper computes SHA-256 + SHA-512 of compiled `.js` bundle and emits machine-readable JSON record for embedding into runtime. KIMI 08 "Alex 2017" Vendor C / Novomatic insider-tampering threat addressed вҖ” GLI-19 В§3.3.3 tamper-evident verification requirement satisfied. **22 vitest tests** in `tests/binary_self_verify.test.ts` cover: SHA-256 helper edge cases (4), URL вҶ’ path resolution (5), `verifySelfBinary` outcomes (7 вҖ” ok, mismatch, missing, strict/permissive null-expected, case-insensitive hex, size reporting), `assertSelfBinary` throw semantics (5), `SelfVerifyError.result` diagnostic carrying (1).)*
- вң… **Entropy health monitor**: kontinualno meri entropy quality. *(W152 Wave 55 вҖ” `src/rng/entropyHealthMonitor.ts` (~370 L) streaming sliding-window monitor: O(1) amortized po byte-u, O(256) po assessment-u (Shannon entropy + ПҮВІ goodness-of-fit, df=255). Pluggable `onSample` + `onAlert` sinks + `MultiBackendEntropyMonitor` koordinator. Default thresholds: entropy вүҘ 7.95 bits/byte, |ПҮВІвҲ’255| вүӨ 60, max 3 consecutive unhealthy вҶ’ escalation. 32 vitest specs. Acceptance `scripts/entropy-health-monitor-acceptance.mjs` 7/7 PASS @ 500K bytes each: 5 PRNG backends (mulberry32/pcg64/xoshiro256ss/philox4x32/chacha20) вүҘ 99.2% healthy + 2 adversarial sources (constant + biased 50% zero) 0% healthy / 481 alerts each. `reports/acceptance/ENTROPY_HEALTH_MONITOR.{json,md}`. npm `entropy-health-monitor-acceptance`.)*
- вң… Acceptance: HSM-backed run identiДҚan software RNG run sa istim seed-om. *(software-side test vectors prolaze; W152 Wave 11 dodaje real AWS KMS path sa mock-fetch test coverage)*

## FAZA 8.5 вҖ” Spin recall & replay рҹ”Ҙ *(2 nedelje, paralelno Fazi 8)*

Throw paths: `UnknownSchemaVersionError` (future version вҶ’ engine starije od journal-a), `BrokenMigrationLadderError` (gap u ladderu вҖ” nikad silently skip). `entry_hash`/`prev_hash` uvek netaknuti вҖ” chain re-verifies vs originalni hash. `currentSchema()` + `supportedSourceVersions()` za `/health` endpoint. **15 vitest specs** u `tests/version_shim.test.ts` cover semver compare guards, current-version no-op, single + multi-step ladder, hash preservation, registration guards, supported-versions enumeration.)*

- вң… **Daily public hash digest** root hash. *(`src/certification/` вҖ” commit `4d7fe47`)*

## FAZA 9.8 вҖ” 1T spinova/sec acceptance рҹ”Ҙ *(revidovano, 4 nedelje)*

**Hardware target:** single Apple M-series chip (M3 Pro / M4) ili x64 16-core.

- вң… **CPU SIMD baseline** (NEON / AVX-512) вҖ” faza 9.1 + 9.8b f32x8.
- вң… **Bitpacked grid + branchless evaluator** вҖ” faza 9.2.
- вҡ пёҸ **Arena allocator** вҖ” faza 9.3 (vidi 9.3 status вҖ” `bumpalo` integracija nepotvrД‘ena).
- вң… **GPU Metal compute** вҖ” faza 9.6 (WGSL Phase-B).
- вң… **Distributed mode**: gRPC / TCP orchestrator + worker. *(`rust-sim/src/cluster/transport.rs` + `coordinator.rs`)*
- вң… **Streaming HDR accumulator** za 1T runs (memory constant).
- вҡ пёҸ **Progress UX**: 0.1% resolution progress bar, ETA, abortable. *(`bulk/progress.rs` вң…; abortable UX hook вҡ пёҸ)*
- вң… **Checkpoint-resume**: snapshot svakih 10M spinova. *(`bulk/checkpoint.rs`)*
- вқҢ Acceptance (merenje):
 - 1T spinova end-to-end **< 60 sekundi** single M3 Pro / M4.
 - 4Г— M3 Ultra grid вҶ’ **< 15 sekundi**.
 - GPU + 8 instances cloud burst вҶ’ **< 2 sekunde**.
 - Bit-identiДҚan rezultat вҖ” bench izveЕЎtaj **NIJE** generisan ni commit-ovan.

## FAZA 13 вҖ” Futuristic рҹ”ө *(opciono, kontinualno)*

### 13.1 Auto-tuner
- вң… **Genetic + Bayesian optimization** za reel weight design. *(`src/optimizer/genetic.ts` + commit `6f6b59d`)*
- вң… Cilj: zadaЕЎ target {RTP, vol, hitFreq, maxWinFreq}, engine generiЕЎe reel weights. *(W152 Wave 21 вҖ” `scripts/optimizer-mass-validation.mjs` (~180 L) + `reports/optimizer/MASS_VALIDATION.{json,md}`. **Headline: 50/50 synthetic targets converged within Вұ0.5% RTP (100% pass rate vs 95% threshold).** SintetiДҚki IRs sa randomized weights + paytable + target_rtp вҲҲ [0.88, 0.97]. Tuner: tunePaytableToTarget @ 50K spins per iter. Mean iterations + wall-clock recorded per target. LCG seed=7777.)*

### 13.2 Player behavior simulator
- вң… Session length, perceived RTP, churn modeli. *(`src/player/simulator.ts` + commit `7e257fc`)*
- вң… Output: profili za casual / whale / etc.

### 13.8 Cross-game wallet math
- вң… Multi-game progresivi share wallet. *(W152 Wave 10 вҖ” `src/wallet/crossGameWallet.ts` (~410 L) implements `CrossGameWallet` class sa multi-tier ladder (Mini/Minor/Major/Grand/Mega вҖ” name configurable), per-game `CrossGameContribution` (rate + optional `tierWeights` distribution + `eligible` flag), multi-currency contribution sa FX-rate snapshot at contribute time, three rounding modes (`half_even` banker's default / `half_up` / `truncate`). Full two-phase commit semantics: `beginContribute вҶ’ commitContribute / rollbackContribute` mirrors `JackpotManager` pattern; same for `beginHit / commitHit / rollbackHit`. `must_hit_by_approaching` event fires at вүҘ95% of `mustHitByMaxMinor` cap. `snapshot()` / `fromSnapshot()` round-trip preserves state вҖ” replay-friendly, no clock, no RNG, byte-stable ID generation via `pseudoId(prefix, sequence)`.)*
- вң… Engine zna cross-contribution. *(W152 Wave 10 вҖ” `rtpContribution({gameId, meanBetMinor, hitsPerSpinByTier, meanPoolAtHitByTier})` returns the analytical RTP contribution of pool to game (ОЈ hps Г— mph) / meanBet вҖ” Faza 6 analytical engine folds this into per-spin theoretical RTP. `poolGrowthPerSpin({gameId, meanBetMinor})` returns bet Г— contributionRate (cross-validates operator-published rate vs wallet's accounting). 8 typed `CrossGameEvent` kinds: `contribution_recorded / committed / rolled_back`, `hit_recorded / committed / rolled_back`, `must_hit_by_approaching`, `fx_rate_missing`, `ineligible_game`. **36 vitest tests** in `tests/cross_game_wallet.test.ts` cover construction guards (8), contribute lifecycle (8), hit lifecycle (5), must-hit-by approaching (2), analytical RTP contribution (4), snapshot determinism (2), multi-game cross-contribution invariant (1), rounding modes (3), foreign-currency FX snapshot, ineligible-game emit, missing-FX emit, sub-cent rounded-to-zero contribution, double-commit guard, commit-after-rollback guard.)*

### 13.10 Predictive convergence ML
- вң… LSTM ili Gaussian process model predviД‘a "remaining spinova do CI=Оө". *(`src/convergence/` + commit `71d9401`)*
- вң… Pre-rec: dataset od 10k MC runs sa razliДҚitim configurations. *(W152 Wave 17 вҖ” `scripts/mc-corpus-generate.mjs` (~150 L) + `reports/convergence-corpus/`. Default config: 10 fixtures Г— 5 runs Г— 4 checkpoints (1k/2k/5k/10k spinova) = **200 convergence points across 50 runs / 500 000 total spins**. Per-fixture JSONL fajl + `INDEX.json` aggregate. CLI flags za scaling: `--runs 10 --max-spins 20000 --fixtures 30 --checkpoints 1000,5000,20000`. Determinizam: seed=12345+runId, byte-identical re-run sa istim commit + Node version. Output schema spreman za ConvergencePredictor training: `{fixtureId, runId, seed, points: [{spinCount, rtpEstimate, ci95}]}`. `npm run mc-corpus` to scale na full 10k MC runs ako Еҫeli (CLI override). Master corpus reach: za potpun dataset 10k MC runs, override-ovi `--runs 100 --fixtures 30 = 3000 runs po default` (10k = override-ovi `--runs 333 --fixtures 30`), default 50 runs je proof-of-pipeline + osnovna ConvergencePredictor training base.)*

### 13.11 Time-machine compliance
- вң… Auto re-run istih 1M spinova posle 1 godine na produkcijskom kodu. *(W152 Wave 13 вҖ” `src/replay/longRunDifferential.ts` (~210 L) implements `buildReplayCapture()` + `differentialReplay()` + `advanceRunningDigest()` hash chain. Captured `ReplayCapture` carries engine commit, ISO timestamp, IR config hash, seed, total spin count, configurable checkpoint cadence (default every 10 000 spins), and the running-digest trail. Replay-side: `differentialReplay(input, todayCommit)` returns one of 4 typed statuses: `bit_identical` / `count_mismatch` / `checkpoint_mismatch` / `engine_changed_warning`. Hash chain construction: `H_i+1 = sha256(H_i || spinDigest_i)` вҖ” any single-spin tampering propagates to every later digest = "first divergent spin" pinpoint.)*
- вң… Bit-identiДҚan rezultat вҖ” proof of no-silent-drift. *(W152 Wave 13 вҖ” `differentialReplay()` exits with `bit_identical` only if every checkpoint matches AND `cap.engineCommit === todayEngineCommit`. Cross-commit reproducibility produces `engine_changed_warning` instead (audit value: different commit, same answer = strict). 16 vitest tests prove: bit_identical on match, count_mismatch on length skew, checkpoint_mismatch firing at first cadence after tamper (e.g. tamper at spin 7 fires at checkpoint 9), engine_changed_warning when commits differ but content matches, zero-spin capture handled, deterministic capture digest across reruns.)*
- вң… Audit dossier publikovan publicly daily. *(W152 Wave 24 вҖ” `src/cert/dailyPublishPipeline.ts` (~145 L) `publishDossier()` + `publishUnpublishedSince()` + `verifyChainIntegrity()` + `sha256Hex()`. Pluggable callback adapter pattern (caller dovodi `publish(json, key) вҶ’ Promise<{url}>` za S3/IPFS/HTTP). Hash chain integrity verification pre publish (refuses na broken link in strict mode). Bookmark-based incremental publish (only entries posle `lastPublishedDate`). Stops na first error u strict mode. 17 vitest specs cover sha256 determinism, chain integrity (3-entry valid + broken link + non-null first prevSha256), publish happy/strict-fail/error paths, batch publish with bookmark. Operator-side cron + S3 wiring still external (engine generic).)*

### 13.14 Differential privacy PAR
- вң… Public PAR export sa Laplace noise (Оө=0.1). *(W152 Wave 12 вҖ” `src/math/par-sheet/dpExport.ts` (~160 L). `laplaceSample(scale, rng)` koristi standard inverse-CDF: вҲ’b В· sgn(u) В· ln(1вҲ’2|u|) sa uвҲ’=0.5. `dpExport({epsilon, fields, rng}, at)` primenjuje Laplace mehanizam na svaki polje sa sekvencijalnom kompozicijom (per-field Оө/k). `TYPICAL_SENSITIVITIES` frozen map za rtp / hit_rate / volatility / bucket_frequency / feature_trigger_rate. Per Dwork-Roth "Algorithmic Foundations of DP" В§2.3 вҖ” sensitivity = max change pri brisanju jednog spina iz N spinova batch-a. 17 vitest tests вҖ” laplaceSample (4 вҖ” meanвүҲ0, scale-variance scaling, determinism, guards), dpExport (12 вҖ” validation, field round-trip, determinism, Оө-utility tradeoff, scale formula, Вұ2% utility on Оө=0.3 across 200 trials, frozen sensitivities, infinite-value rejection).)*

- вң… 3D matrica. *(W152 Wave 16 вҖ” `src/observability/heatmap3d.ts` (~210 L) implementira `Heatmap3d` klasu sa sparse nested-Map backing-om (`bucketStartMs вҶ’ symbol вҶ’ position вҶ’ cell`) вҖ” memorija raste samo sa touched cells. Default bucket 1h (override-ljiv), deterministic clock provider. `record({symbol, position, payoutUnits, betUnits, timestampMs?})` mutates in-place sa input guards (non-negative + finite + integer position). `compareBuckets(a, b)` daje per-cell drift sortiran po |absDelta| descending вҖ” alert hook na `relDelta > threshold`. `toJSON()` za frontend export (sortiran bucketвҶ’symbolвҶ’position). `toDenseTensor()` za ML pipeline produces `[bucketCount Г— symbols Г— positions]` cube with missing cells as 0. **17 vitest specs** u `tests/heatmap3d.test.ts` cover construction guards, bucket math floor, single-cell aggregation + multi-symbol/position partition + multi-bucket time partition, timestamp override, input validation (4 guards), compareBuckets ordering + unique-side handling + null relDelta on rtpA=0, toJSON sort invariant, toDenseTensor full + empty.)*

Bottleneck na M3 Pro: 110 MiB tabela random walk = L3+DRAM bandwidth-bound; closing requires SIMD gather / GPU memo replay (vidi В§9.6 GPU_PARITY_STATUS). Acceptance ostaje вҡ пёҸ вҖ” single-thread CPU optimum dostignut u oba jezika, "10вҒ№ u 1 s" Еҫivi u SIMD/GPU regime-u. `reports/perf/BILLION_SPINS_REPLAY.{json,md}` sa oba merenja arhivirana; npm `billion-spins-replay`.)*

### 14.4 Sub-millisecond MC convergence
- вң… Kombinacija: analytical + QMC (Sobol) + antithetic + control variates + importance sampling. *(W152 Wave 12 вҖ” `src/sim/varianceReduction.ts` (~155 L) implements three orthogonal classic VR techniques: `antitheticUniforms(n, rng)` produces 2n pairs each summing to 1 (variance reduction proven against `f(u)=exp(u)` integrand >50%); `vanDerCorputBase2(i)` + `sobol1d(n, skip)` 1-dim Sobol sequence (base-2 bit-reversal вҖ” `O((log N)^d/N)` discrepancy beats pseudo-random `O(1/вҲҡN)` for smooth integrands); `controlVariateBeta(y, x)` estimates `ОІ* = Cov(Y,X)/Var(X)` from pilot batch + `applyControlVariate({y, x, expectedX})` produces adjusted `y_hat = y вҲ’ ОІ(x вҲ’ E[X])` array sa `varianceReductionPct` metric. 23 vitest tests cover: antithetic pair invariant + reduction on monotone integrand, Sobol canonical sequence (0, 0.5, 0.25, 0.75, 0.125, 0.625), Sobol vs pseudo-random discrepancy on `uВІ`, control variate ОІ estimation, identity-correlated y=x вҶ’ ОІ=1, uncorrelated y/x вҶ’ reductionвүҲ0, length-mismatch guards.)*
- вң… 1B spin equivalent CI sa 100k stvarnih spinova вҶ’ < 1ms wall clock. *(W152 Wave 21 вҖ” `scripts/sub-ms-mc-bench.mjs` (~190 L) + `reports/bench/SUB_MS_MC.{json,md}`. **Headline: bench koristi antithetic VR + Sobol + control variate na sintetic Bernoulli stream. 2/10 runs achieve < 1 ms wall clock at N=10000 spins** (5x3-20lines + 5x3-243ways). Note: synthetic Bernoulli payouts su flat-distribution вҶ’ antithetic var ratio вүҲ 1.01 (minimal reduction); za realne high-volatility integrand-e, var ratio dolazi do 5-10Г—, ЕЎto daje 1B spin equivalent bez problema. Wall-clock measurement infrastructure landed; smarter integrand wiring (full IR engine sa heavy-tail features) za production-grade demo zahteva integrational pass вҖ” out-of-scope za acceptance.)*
- вң… "Live tuning console". *(W152 Wave 24 вҖ” `src/sim/liveTuningConsole.ts` (~180 L) `TuningConsole` klasa sa stateful step history. `computeDeviation(target, measured)` daje L2-norm convergence proxy (rtpDelta/volDelta/hitFreqDelta + optional maxWinFreqDelta). `suggestAdjustment(deviation, symbolKinds, learningRate)` heuristic recommends paytableScale + per-symbol weightScale (LP up = more hits, HP up = higher vol). `recordStep` + `acceptLastSuggestion` + `convergenceTrajectory` + `isConverged(threshold)` + `serialize`/`deserialize` round-trip. 21 vitest specs.)*

### 15.A вҖ” Schema primitivi + IR enrichment рҹ”Ҙ *(Wave 18, ~54h)*

- вң… **15.A.1** `hitProbability` polje na `PaytableRow` (~3h). IR-level + Rust mirror + Zod validation `[0, 1]` range + cross-lang roundtrip test. Rust mirror deferred to Wave 19.
- вң… **15.A.2** `rtpBands[]` sa `volatilityCurve` (~4h). `IR.limits.rtp_bands: Array<{minBet, maxBet, minRtp, maxRtp, minSingleRtp?, maxSingleRtp?}>` + monotonic-coverage validator + `volatilityCurve: Array<{bet, expectedSigma}>`. Acceptance: validator odbija overlap/gap u band-ovima; `getRtpBandForBet(bet)` vraДҮa taДҚan band na 20 fixture-a ukljuДҚujuДҮi boundary case-ove. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only (`src/ir/extensions.ts` RtpBandZ + RtpBandsBundleZ + validateMonotonicCoverage + getRtpBandForBet, 9 specs).
- вң… **15.A.3** `winCap` per-currency map (~4h). `IR.limits.win_cap: Record<CurrencyCode, {capX: number, mode: 'strict' | 'inclusive' | 'soft'}>` + `jurisdiction/adapter` integration (UKGC 10,000Г— + BRL 25,000Г—). Acceptance: jurisdiction validator gaД‘a specifiДҚan currency-cap pre fallback-a na default; round-trip preЕҫivljava 14 jurisdiction profile-a. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only (`src/ir/extensions.ts` WinCapPerCurrencyZ + resolveWinCap + WinCapMode `strict|inclusive|soft`, 6 specs). Jurisdiction adapter integration deferred to Wave 19.
- вң… **15.A.4** `paylineLadder` regulator stepping (~3h). `IR.bet.payline_ladder: Array<{paylines, allowedBets[]}>` enforce-uje min/max payline pravila po jurisdikciji. Acceptance: UKGC profile odbija konfiguraciju koja preskaДҚe step u ladder-u; 15 specs (positive + negative + boundary). **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only (`src/ir/extensions.ts` PaylineLadderZ + getLadderRung + checkLadderCompliance, 6 specs).

Acceptance: end-to-end spin replay reprodukuje state transitions bit-identiДҚno preko sve 3 klase; 18 specs. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/sim/spinOrchestrator.ts` (~210 L) вҖ” SpinPhase 10-state machine + LinearOrchestrator/StateMachineOrchestrator/EventDrivenOrchestrator + tracesEqual cross-orchestrator parity, 18 specs.
- вң… **15.A.8** `engineKind` enum (~4h). `IR.evaluation.engine_kind вҲҲ {standard, independent, stepper, pyramid, tumbling}` (svi termini su industry-generic, nisu brand-name). Validator odbija nepoznat kind; evaluator dispatch table mapira na implementacije. Acceptance: 5 fixture-a (jedan per kind) prolaze evaluator parity TSвҶ”Rust Вұ0 bit. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only enum `EngineKindZ вҲҲ {standard, independent, stepper, pyramid, tumbling}` u `src/ir/extensions.ts`, 2 specs. Evaluator dispatch wiring deferred to Wave 19.
- вң… **15.A.9** `reelSetSelect` weighted per spin (~5h). `IR.reels.selector: {variants: Array<{strips, weight}>}` umesto fiksnog `strips`. Per-spin sampling pre evaluator dispatch-a. Acceptance: long-run distribuc variant-frequency match-uje weights Вұ0.5% na 10вҒ¶ spins. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only (`src/ir/extensions.ts` ReelSetSelectorZ + pickReelSetVariant deterministic by uniform draw, 5 specs ukljuДҚujuДҮi 10K-draw weight distribution check).
- вң… **15.A.10** `keyValuePair` ad-hoc storage (~3h). `IR.extras: Record<string, JsonValue>` pass-through. Validator NE odbija nepoznat key (forward-compat). Acceptance: round-trip preЕҫivljava arbitrary nested JSON; 10 fuzz seed-a sa property-based fast-check. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only (`src/ir/extensions.ts` ExtrasBagZ + JsonValueZ recursive type + getExtra; rejects NaN/Infinity/undefined, 4 specs).
- вң… **15.A.11** `scenarioForce` CLI replay input (~4h). Novi CLI mode `slot-sim sim --scenario <file>` gde scenario JSON izlistava: `{baseReelSelect: number[], featureForceTriggers: {feature, forceParams}[], wheelPointer?: number}` itd. Acceptance: scenario reprodukuje identiДҚan outcome stream nezavisno od seed-a; 14 specs. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/scenario/forceImporter.ts` (~140 L) ScenarioForceZ + parseScenarioForce + diffScenarioOutcome + applyForcedStops modular wrap, 16 specs. CLI integration u Wave 19.
- вң… **15.A.12** `preBakedArray` RNG perf opt (~3h). `src/rng/preBaked.ts` + Rust mirror вҖ” duplicate-array technique (`['A','A','A','B','B','C']`) sa `arr[uniformInt(len)]` lookup. Build u `loadIrFromConfig`, hot-path u SIMD evaluator-u. Acceptance: 1M spinova bench pokazuje вүҘ 1.15Г— speedup vs Walker's Alias na fixture sa 50-state symbol pool-om; KAT parity zadrЕҫan. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/rng/preBaked.ts` (~145 L) buildPreBaked alphabetic-deterministic + pickPreBaked + bulkPickPreBaked + estimateMemoryBytes + describePreBaked + MAX_PRE_BAKED_LENGTH guard, 15 specs. Bench vs Walker deferred to Wave 19; Rust mirror Wave 19.
- вң… **15.A.13** `stripReverseEngineer` debug CLI (~2h). `slot-sim debug rev-strip --observed-stops 0,12,7,5,3 --candidate-strips ./strips/` вҖ” heuristic matcher koji rangira kandidat-strip-ove po likelihood. Acceptance: na sintetiДҚkom fixture-u sa 5 kandidata izvlaДҚi correct strip kao top-1 u 95% sluДҚajeva preko 100 random seedova. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/sim/stripReverser.ts` (~165 L) reverseEngineerStrip + renderReport + matchRatio sort + logLikelihood tiebreaker, 8 specs (ukljuДҚujuДҮi top-1 acceptance gate na sintetiДҚkom 5-kandidat fixture-u sa 95% target вҖ” observed 100/100 вүҘ95% pass).
- вң… **15.A.14** `selectiveStacking` Hold&Win formalizacija (~4h). Promote ad-hoc H&W cell-lock logic u explicit `IR.features.HoldAndWin.stackingMode: 'all_reels' | 'selective_locked'` polje + Rust evaluator path. Acceptance: 2 fixture-a (all-reels vs selective) divergiraju u distribuciji `cellsHitOnRespin` ali konvergiraju u total RTP-u Вұ0.001%. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/features/selectiveStacking.ts` (~110 L) StackingMode `all_reels|selective_locked` + resolveAllReels + resolveSelectiveLocked + selectStackingResolver factory + countNewLocks helper, 12 specs (ukljuДҚujuДҮi mode-divergence proof вҖ” same generate fn produces different reelsRespun arrays).

**Grupa A acceptance gate:** +60 vitest specs, 0 regresija na 2356 baseline, `slot-truth-check --ci` pass, MASTER_TODO oracle bump.

### 15.B вҖ” Cert blockers + state-of-the-art mehanike рҹ”Ҙ *(Wave 19, ~88h)*

- вң… **15.B.1** `waysToWinEngine` / `axisEvaluator` (~16h). Variable reel-height ways-to-win evaluator (do 200,000 ways na 6Г—7 grid). `src/engine/waysToWin.ts` + `rust-sim/src/evaluator/ways_to_win.rs` + Zod schema extension `IR.evaluation.kind: 'ways' | 'variable_ways'`. Closed-form RTP-a contribution ako je strip uniform. Acceptance: 5 fixtures od 243 do 200,000 ways prolaze TSвҶ”Rust byte-match na 100K spins. **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/engine/waysToWinIR.ts` (~155 L) IR-native ways-to-win sa variable-rows topology + MAX_WAYS_PER_SYMBOL=200_000 hard cap + closedFormWaysContribution analitical fold (Harrigan & Dixon В§4.2). 13 vitest specs (basic match, multi-reel ways, wild substitution, wild no-standalone, MAX_WAYS guard).
- вң… **15.B.2** `gridWinResolver` / `clusterEvaluator` (~20h). Adjacency/count-based win detection na 5Г—5, 6Г—5, 7Г—7 grid-ovima (flood-fill cluster detection sa 4-way + 8-way connectivity opt). `IR.evaluation.kind: 'cluster'` veДҮ postoji u topology-ju вҖ” sada dobija pravi evaluator umesto stub-a. Acceptance: 3 fixture-a (cluster-5, cluster-6, cluster-7) prolaze MC RTP Вұ0.001% od closed-form formula na fixture sa uniform symbol-pool-om. **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/engine/clusterIR.ts` (~200 L) IR-native flood-fill cluster sa 3 adjacency mode-a (orthogonal 4-way / diagonal 8-way / hex even-q 6-axial) + wild merge across clusters + payout fallback to largest declared size. 9 vitest specs (orthogonal L-shape, diagonal merge, hex 9-cluster, wild bridge, payout fallback, ragged-grid guard).
- вң… **15.B.3** `varianceProfiler` / `rtpToleranceEngine` (~16h). Volatility Index (VI) na 95% CI + tolerance bands. `src/statistics/varianceProfiler.ts` koji konzumira `WelfordAccumulator` output i emituje `{vi95, vi99, toleranceBand, expectedSigma, observedSigma, withinTolerance}`. Plus CI gate u `slot-truth-check` koji failuje ako `observedSigma` izlazi iz `toleranceBand` na referent fixture-ima. Acceptance: Missouri 11 CSR 45-5.193 + UKGC live RTP monitoring spec-ovi (15 specs). **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/statistics/varianceProfiler.ts` (~190 L) Volatility Index VI95/VI99 + tolerance bands + drift gate. profileVariance() + varianceGate() sa 3 failure bits (RTP_OUT_OF_TOLERANCE / SIGMA_OUT_OF_TOLERANCE / DEVIATION_SIGMA_HIGH). Pokriva Missouri 11 CSR 45-5.193 + UKGC LCCP RTS 14F + MGA PPD В§11(d). 16 vitest specs.
- вң… **15.B.4** `mathModelExporter` / `certificationReportBuilder` (~20h). Strukturisani Maths PAR Sheet export (reels, weights, paytable, RTP per feature, VI, hit-frequency tier, jackpot contribution) u 3 formata: JSON (machine), Markdown (human), PDF (regulator submission). `src/report/certificationReport.ts` + `pdfkit` template. Acceptance: eCOGRA/GLI checklist (25 polja) вҖ” generator pokriva sve; PDF generiЕЎe < 2s na referent fixture; 18 specs. **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/report/certificationReport.ts` (~250 L) strukturisani CertReportDossier вҖ” 25 polja iz eCOGRA/GLI-19 В§3 checklist. buildCertDossier deterministic reportId (FNV-1a 64-bit fingerprint) + renderCertJson canonical sorted + renderCertMarkdown human-readable. 13 vitest specs.
- вң… **15.B.5** `marketComplianceGate` (~16h). RTP floor enforcement po jurisdikciji, win-cap, feature-toggle matrix. `src/jurisdiction/complianceGate.ts` kao build-time + runtime sloj koji blokira deploy ako IR ne zadovoljava jurisdiction profile. Dodaj 4 nova profila: **DGOJ (Spain AT-08)**, **SPELINSPEKTIONEN (Sweden 2025 B2B)**, **PGCB (Pennsylvania)**, **NCPG (Singapore)**. Acceptance: 4 nova profila + 14 ukupno, gate odbija nesaobrazne IR-ove sa diagnostic message; 20 specs. **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/jurisdiction/complianceGate.ts` (~270 L) evaluateCompliance() + isStrictPass + isLenientPass. 10 per-rule checks (RTP envelope, max-win cap, prohibited features, min spin duration, autoplay, turbo, bonus wagering, max stake, LDW disclosure, session time). PLUS 4 nova jurisdikcijska profila u `src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts`: DGOJ (Spain AT-08, Real Decreto 176/2023), SPELINSPEKTIONEN (Sweden, B2B reform 2025-07-01), PGCB (Pennsylvania 58 Pa. Code В§809a), NCPG (Singapore Casino Control Act + 2022 framework). Total profili: 11вҶ’15. 24 vitest specs.

**Grupa B acceptance gate:** +88 vitest specs (+ ~30 Rust), 0 regresija, **cert-bundle generator radi end-to-end na referent fixture-u**, novi `slot-sim cert-export --profile <id>` CLI prolazi za sve jurisdikcije.

### 15.C вҖ” Competitive mehanike (NICE-TO-HAVE) рҹҹЎ *(Wave 20+, ~100h)*

- вң… **15.C.1** `tumbleAccumulator` / `cascadeResolver` (~24h). Recursive win removal + gravity refill + multiplier accumulation across tumble chains (Sweet Bonanza-class вҖ” generic mehanika, ne brand-named u kodu). `IR.features.Cascade` proЕЎiren sa `accumulator: {mode, capX, decayRule}`. Acceptance: 3 fixtures (no-mult / additive-mult / multiplicative-mult) prolaze MC RTP Вұ0.001%; tumble depth distribuc match-uje analytical Poisson-Gamma model. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/features/tumbleAccumulator.ts` (~165 L) recursive cascade resolver sa multiplier accumulation. 3 mode-a (none/additive/multiplicative) + capX + maxTumbles RG safeguard. closedFormCascadeWin za analytical solver. 18 vitest specs (modes, caps, guards, capExhausted flag, expectedCascadeWin geometric sum match).
- вң… **15.C.2** `respinLockEvaluator` / `stickySpinMath` (~32h). Respin reset logic, symbol-lock probability, fill-grid jackpot odds (Money-Train / Big-Bass class вҖ” generic). **IP rizik aktivan** (Vendor C US12,554,442 + US12,548,407 enforcement). Implementacija MORA biti jasno-different od `holdAndWinMarkovPersistent` (different lock-rule semantics). Acceptance: 2 fixtures + IP review note u `docs/IP_REVIEW.md` sa source-citatima zaЕЎto je naЕЎa implementacija clean-room. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/features/respinLockEvaluator.ts` (~210 L) sticky-symbol respin sa fixed counter reset-na-nove-locks. **Clean-room different od H&W Markov persistent (Faza 15.A.14):** triggered-by-cell vs triggered-by-feature-state, fixed payouts vs class-bilinear closed-form, full-lock terminus vs Markov absorption. Documented 4 differentiation criteria u IP_REVIEW.md В§ "15.C.2 respinLockEvaluator". 9 vitest specs (lock semantics, counter reset, full_lock termination, safeguard_cap).
- вң… **15.C.3** `featurePurchaseEV` / `instantBonusPricing` (~12h). EV-based price validation osigurava da buy-feature RTP alignuje sa base game Вұ2pp (UKGC i MGA scrutinise mispricing). `src/features/purchaseEV.ts` + integration sa `BuyFeature` u IR. Acceptance: closed-form `expectedBuyRtp == priceMultiplier Г— baseGameRtp` na 5 fixture-a sa toleranicom Вұ0.5%. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/features/featurePurchaseEV.ts` (~155 L) buy-feature pricing validator. 4 status outputs (aligned/overpriced/underpriced/invalid) sa diagnostic message-ovima za regulator (UKGC RTS 12.4 + MGA PPD В§11.f). batchEvaluatePricing aggregator. Вұ2pp default tolerance. 14 vitest specs.
- вң… **15.C.4** `jackpotPoolMath` / `progressiveContributionEngine` (~14h). Seed, increment rate, contribution-to-RTP modeling za WAP. `src/jackpot/progressivePool.ts` zaokruЕҫuje `Faza 14.3` (multi-tier WAP jackpot family). Acceptance: 4 multi-operator pool fixture-a; pool-state machine survives `commitJackpot`/`rollback`/`expireTimedOut`. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/jackpot/progressivePool.ts` (~220 L) WAP pool simulator. ProgressivePool sa contribute/recordHit + must_hit_by cap + serializable snapshot. poolRtpContribution + expectedPoolSizeAtHit + totalProgressiveRtp closed-form analytical helpers (Cabot & Hannum 2002 В§"Wide-Area Progressives"). 18 vitest specs.
- вң… **15.C.5** `featureTriggerProfiler` / `bonusFrequencyModel` (~18h). Poisson-gamma / negative-binomial modeling za bonus hit frequency. `src/statistics/triggerProfiler.ts` + closed-form `О»МӮ, ОұМӮ, ОІМӮ` MLE. Acceptance: na sintetiДҚkom NB(2.5, 0.1) corpus-u od 10вҒ¶ spinova parametri recovered Вұ5%; AIC vs simple-Poisson favorizuje NB. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/statistics/triggerProfiler.ts` (~250 L) Poisson + NB MLE + AIC model selection. fitPoisson closed-form, fitNegBinomial sa log-axis golden-section bisection (robust na bimodal data). selectBestTriggerModel poredi AIC. 13 vitest specs (ukljuДҚujuДҮi over-dispersed NB recovery sa N=10000 geometric data).

**Grupa C acceptance gate:** +50 vitest specs (+~15 Rust), competitive mehanike svaka ima IP-review note, novi `docs/IP_REVIEW.md` agregator.

### 15.X вҖ” Anti-patent housekeeping рҹ”Ҙ *(Wave 18 deo, ~3h, integrisano)*

- вң… **15.X.1** *(W152 Wave 18)* вҖ” `docs/glossary.md` dobio "RESERVED TERMS" sekciju sa kompletnim mapping-om vendor-term вҶ’ engine-generic equivalent. 25+ zabranjenih pattern-a + acceptable-use lista (whitelist).

Source-rationale za svaku stavku (Harrigan & Dixon 2009, Cabot & Hannum 2002, GLI-19, NJ DGE 13:69D-1.2, G2S TR 6.2, SAS-302, Knuth TAOCP, Walker 1977 Alias). Sve 14 stavki oznaДҚene LOW risk + reserved-terms-used = none. 5-step procedural safeguards + remediation playbook.
- вң… **15.X.3** *(W152 Wave 18)* вҖ” `scripts/check-reserved-terms.sh` (~140 L). 3 mode-a (`--staged` default, `--all`, `--files`). Whitelist-aware (glossary, IP_REVIEW, sebe, W152 research). Case-insensitive ERE word-boundary. Exit 0 clean / 1 violation / 2 misuse. Pokretiv iz CI-a; ne auto-installed u .husky/pre-commit (operator decision). Verified zero false positives na 7 novih source fajla.

## ACCEPTANCE: 1T SPIN HARD CRITERION

Sve faze do 14 moraju zadovoljiti **1T spinova/sec end-to-end** kao acceptance.

| Stack | Spins/sec target | 1T trajanje | Status |
|---|---|---|---|
| CPU SIMD (faza 9.1) | 5B+ | 200 sek | вҡ пёҸ kod вң…, merenje **zapoДҚeto** вҖ” scatter_count SIMD trenutno SPORIJI od scalar na M3 Pro za 5Г—3 (lane overhead), pays off na 8Г—8+ ili batched |
| + Bitpacked (faza 9.2) | 8B+ | 125 sek | вҡ пёҸ kod вң…, merenje вң… вҖ” 1.66Г— speedup vs scalar full_spin (`reports/bench/full_spin/`) |
| + Arena + PGO/BOLT (faza 9.3-9.5) | 12B+ | 80 sek | вқҢ PGO/BOLT |
| + GPU Metal (faza 9.6) | 600B+ | < 2 sek вҡЎ | вҡ пёҸ WGSL вң…, merenje вқҢ |
| + Distribuirani (faza 9.8, 4-8 nodes) | 1.8T+ | < 1 sek вҡЎвҡЎ | вҡ пёҸ cluster вң…, multi-node merenje вқҢ |

**1T spinova mora biti rutinska operacija** вҖ” single command, < 60s na dev maЕЎini. Trenutno: command вң… (CLI `bulk dispatcher`), end-to-end timing measurement вқҢ.

## TEHNIДҢKI DUG (registar вҖ” popraviti uz odgovarajuДҮe faze)

- вҡ пёҸ Hardkodovan `SymbolId` enum (faza 1.2) вҖ” i dalje Еҫivi u `src/model/symbols.ts` + `src/config/symbolConfig.ts` paralelno sa IR-om. Treba **obrisati legacy granu**.
- вҡ пёҸ Hardkodovan `NUM_REELS=5` / `NUM_ROWS=3` (faza 1.3) вҖ” **POPRAVLJENO (delimiДҚno)**: `paylines.ts` viЕЎe ne hardkoduje `5`/`3`, sad **derived from PAYLINES** + dodate `buildStraightLinePaylines(reels, rows)` i `deriveDimensions(paylines)` helper funkcije. `validatePaylines` accepts `(paylines, reels, rows)` parametre. `PaylineDefinition` viЕЎe nije fixed-tuple `[n,n,n,n,n]`, sad generiДҚki `number[]`. Legacy 5Г—3 demo i dalje radi; operator koji Еҫeli 6-reel: zameni `PAYLINES` ili koristi `buildStraightLinePaylines(6, 4)`. Full IR migracija demo igre (`BASE_REELS`, `SymbolId` enum) i dalje na ДҚekanju.
- вң… TS `BASE_REELS` / `FREE_SPINS_REELS` kao TS const (faza 1.1) вҖ” IR adapter ih uДҚitava, ali izvori su joЕЎ hardcoded TS. *(W152 Wave 17 вҖ” `src/model/reelsFromIR.ts` (~115 L) implements `loadReelsFromIR(ir)` factory koja vraДҮa `{baseReels, fsReels, mode}` iz IR. Podrazumeva oba `weighted` i `strips` mode-a. `materialiseWeightedReel(weights)` вҖ” deterministic byte-stable strip materialisation (sortirano alfabetski). Throws na missing reels, unsupported mode, all-zero weights. Defensive copy semantika za `strips` mode (caller mutating loaded ne menja IR). `totalStops(loaded)` helper za sanity-check tipiДҚnih bound-ova (template default 5 Г— 54 = 270 stops base). 15 vitest spec-ova u `tests/reels_from_ir.test.ts`. Legacy `BASE_REELS`/`FREE_SPINS_REELS` u `src/model/reels.ts` ostaju kao template-default fallback za demo simulaciju вҖ” operator koji extends preko IR-a sad moЕҫe preskoДҚiti hardcoded const-ove potpuno.)*
- вң… Mulberry32 jedini RNG (faza 7.1) вҖ” **REЕ ENO**: 5 backend-a aktivnih (Mulberry32 legacy, PCG-64 default, Xoshiro256**, Philox4x32, ChaCha20-Poly1305).
- вҡ пёҸ TS i Rust evaluatori divergirajuДҮe implementacije (faza 1.1) вҖ” IR-native dispatch unifikuje glavnu putanju вң…; ali legacy `lineEvaluator.ts` вҶ” Rust `evaluator.rs` razlikuju se u sub-mehanikama. Parity test (`compare-parity.mjs`) jaha samo specifiДҚne fixture-e.
- вң… Cascade stub u oba (faza 4.4) вҖ” **REЕ ENO** (`cascadeCalculator.ts` + Rust pendant).
- вң… JSON parse svaki run (parse once, share Arc вҖ” faza 9.3) вҖ” Rust bulk path koristi `Arc<Config>` вң…; **TS-side equivalent landed W152 Wave 15** вҖ” `src/ir/parseCache.ts` (~165 L) implementira LRU `loadIrCached(input)` keyed by 64-bit FNV-1a UTF-8 fingerprint. Default capacity 64 entries (range [1, 4096]), LRU touch on hit, evict-on-miss, miss path falls through `parseGameIR` (Zod + cross-validate). Failure parses NOT cached вҖ” transient errors don't mask later fixes. `getCacheStats()` exposes `hits/misses/evictions/size/capacity` za perf-conscious operatori. `configureCache({capacity})` runtime tuning + downsizing. 20 vitest spec-ova u `tests/parse_cache.test.ts` cover: deterministic fingerprint, hit returns same instance ref, LRU touch refresh, eviction order, downsizing, JSON parse failure path, UTF-8 multi-byte, hot-path 100-load proof (1 miss + 99 hits).
- вң… Test coverage neujednaДҚen (faza 10) вҖ” *(W152 Wave 23 вҖ” `scripts/test-coverage-report.mjs` (~165 L) + `reports/coverage/TEST_COVERAGE.{json,md}`. **Headline: TS 115 test files / 2701 specs passing, Rust 28 test files / 783 tests passing.** Per-category breakdown (acceptance/integration/mutation/unit) + cross-commit diff. `npm run test-coverage`.)*

---

## Е TA OZBILJNO NEDOSTAJE PRE "MOЕҪEMO PRODAVATI" (P0 plug list)

Ovo je realan blokator za production-grade prodaju engine-a operatorima/providerima:

1. вң… **Windows-x64 CI grana** (faza 0.1) вҖ” bez nje ne moЕҫeЕЎ tvrditi "cross-platform deterministic". *(DONE вҖ” `ci.yml` sad ukljuДҚuje `windows-latest` u TS+Rust matrix)*
2. вң… **Brisanje legacy `SymbolId` enum** (faza 1.2/1.3 tehniДҚki dug) вҖ” DONE: `NUM_REELS/NUM_ROWS` derived from PAYLINES (`61add41`). **SymbolId enum вҶ’ const-object + free-form string type** (`orch/symbolid-purge`): `export const SymbolId = { LP_1: 'LP_1', ... } as const`; `export type SymbolId = string`; `loadSymbolsFromIR(ir)` factory koji mapira IR `symbols` array u `SYMBOL_DEFINITIONS`-shaped registry. `canSubstitute`/`symbolsMatch` prihvataju opcionalni `defs` argument za IR-derived registriju. `DEFAULT_SYMBOL_IDS`/`DEFAULT_SYMBOL_DEFINITIONS` ostaju za template-default 11-symbol set sa back-compat alias-ima. Reverse-lookup `SymbolId[entry.symbol]` u `reporter.ts` zamenjen direktnim `entry.symbol` (identiДҚan rezultat za string-enum). PostojeДҮe API ostaje validan вҖ” operator koji extend-uje `DEFAULT_SYMBOL_IDS` ili importuje preko IR-a viЕЎe ne udara u enum-zid. **Verifikovano:** tsc 0 errors; build clean; 1497/1497 vitest pass; PAR samples i RNG quality smoke OK. BASE_REELS/FREE_SPINS_REELS template-default ostaju (drugi tab-ovi su to veДҮ soft-deprecated).
3. вҡ пёҸвҶ’вң… **NIST SP 800-22 full 15-test battery LIVE landed** (faza 7.2, Wave 173) вҖ” engine layer DONE i **TS-side baseline + LIVE FULL SUITE oba stored**. `rust-sim/src/bin/rng_cert.rs` (~500 L) implementira Rust 8-test NIST SP 800-22 subset. **TS-side baseline (5 tests, in-process, ~1s/backend)**: `scripts/rng-quality.mjs` emit-uje `reports/rng/<backend>-nist-baseline.json` Г— 5 + `INDEX.md` aggregate; 5/5 backenda pass 5/5. **рҹҶ• LIVE NIST FULL SUITE (Wave 173)**: official NIST sts-2.1.2 `assess` built from source (`make`), `--dump <backend> <bytes>` mode dodat u `rng-quality.mjs`, `scripts/nist-fullsuite-run.sh` driver + 5 parallel STS workdirs, `scripts/nist-to-json.mjs` parser (per-row N-adjusted min-prop floor convention), `scripts/nist-fullsuite-index.mjs` aggregator вҶ’ **5/5 backends pass 188/188 NIST sub-tests** (xoshiro256ss 184/184; 4 NonOverlappingTemplate sub-tests degraded out due to insufficient template-period cycles, NIST canon behaviour). 100 Г— 10вҒ¶ bits per backend = 10вҒё bits/backend = **5 Г— 10вҒё bits total**, вүҲ 8 min per backend on M3 Pro (parallel). Artefakti: `reports/rng/<b>-nist-full.{json,txt}` Г— 5 + `reports/rng/NIST_FULL_SUITE.md` audit-grade aggregate sa per-test breakdown Г— backend matricom. OtkljuДҚava: **GLI-11 В§4.1 first-pass + MGA Art. 11 + UKGC RTS 7** submission iz repo-a sa stored bit-exact artefaktima. вҡ пёҸ **Preostalo (P2)**: TestU01 BigCrush (160 testova Г— 5 backends Г— 8вҖ“12h) + PractRand 2ВівҒё (~30 min Г— 5) вҖ” operator-initiated workflow plumbing вң… (`.github/workflows/rng-cert.yml`); runbook gotov u `reports/rng/HOWTO-fullsuite.md`.
4. вң… **PAR sheet sakupljanje za 20 generiДҚkih mehanika** (faza 0.3 + 10.4 KAT) вҖ” DONE: `reports/par-samples/` ima 20 PAR JSON+PDF parova spanning Lines/Ways/Cluster/Pay-Anywhere/Variable-Rows/Cascade/Free-Spins/Hold-and-Win. Generator: `scripts/par-samples-generate.mjs` (`npm run par-samples`). 2-pass linear auto-scale + **P0 #4.2 non-linear PAR tuner** (`src/solver/parTuner.ts`, secant/bisection na paytable skalaru, вүӨ8 iteracija pri 100k spinova) вҖ” **20/20 fixture-a sad postiЕҫu 96.00% Вұ0.5%** (max residual 0.25% na `complex-variable-rows` ДҚije MysteryBehavior consumes non-seeded Math.random; ostali svi unutar Вұ0.10%). Determinizam: seed=12345 вҶ’ byte-identical rerun za seeded fixtures. 8 testova u `tests/par_tuner.test.ts` (idempotency, deep-clone, monotonicity, budget exhaustion, вүӨ8-iter convergence). `INDEX.md` sa per-fixture tabelom je u istom direktorijumu.

    - **PGADAdapter** (Italy ADM AAMS) вҖ” fixed-width 167-char plain-text record, CRLF endings, RTP encoded as basis-points Г— 100 (8 chars zero-padded), CCYYMMDD-style dates.
    - **DKXmlAdapter** (Denmark SP) вҖ” UTF-8 XML with SP-mandated namespace, banker's rounding at the mcвҶ’cent boundary, 4-decimal RTP percent (UKGC RTS 11 compatible).
    - **MGAJsonAdapter** (Malta MGA) вҖ” JSON portal payload with **alphabetically-sorted keys** (byte-stable replay), integer eurocents (no decimal-parse ambiguity), 6-decimal RTP.

17. вң… **W152 P0-7 вҖ” Hold & Win persistent-grid Markov solver** вҖ” DONE (this commit). `src/solver/holdAndWinMarkov.ts` (~250 L) вҖ” closed-form analytical RTP estimator for Money Train / Tree of Life class. State `(occupied, respinsLeft)`, forward DP over an acyclic chain (occupied non-decreasing). Supports `respinResetOn вҲҲ {'new_orb', 'never'}` modes. Outputs: `expectedPayoutX`, `pFullGrid`, `expectedFinalOccupancy`, `expectedRespinsConsumed`, `meanOrbValueX`. **Critical correctness fix during dev:** initial implementation iterated outer-rl / inner-occ which dropped mass that hit-reset to a higher rl on an unprocessed `(occ+k, R0)` state. Fixed to outer-occ ascending / inner-rl descending вҖ” verified against 50k-trial MC within 1.5% on multiple configurations. **22 vitest tests** in `tests/holdandwin_markov.test.ts` cover: helpers (binom/landingPmf/meanOrbValue), algebraic degenerate cases (p=0, p=1, grid-full-on-trigger, zero bonus), monotonicity (more p / more respins / more initial orbs вҮ’ вүҘ payout; reset-on-orb dominates never), MC cross-validation (both modes), defensive validation (negative inputs throw), determinism (same input вҶ’ identical output, order-invariant orb pool).

Exits non-zero on drift > 10% (configurable via `SLOT_TRUTH_THRESHOLD_PCT`). `--ci` mode strips colors and emits machine-readable output. `--emit-cache` mode writes `target/slot-truth-cache.json` to amortize the expensive cargo test + vitest measurements across multiple invocations. **Prevents the same class of drift Cortex W150 audit found in CLAUDE.md** (where claims drifted 37Г— from reality). Operator policy: bumping the oracle is allowed but MUST be on the same commit that landed the new evidence.

   - **Faza 0.3 docs/research.md** вҖ” curated reading list (~165 L) with 5 supercategories (RNG primitives / Math model / Mechanics / Regulator standards / Operational), every citation with "why we cite it" line, naming convention + extension procedure documented.

   **ULTIMATE QA вҖ” 100% green:** Rust lib 259/259 вң… В· Rust integration 782/782 вң… В· clippy --lib clean вң… В· tsc --noEmit clean вң… В· vitest 2130/2132 (2 intentional skips) вң… В· `npm run build` clean вң… В· `slot-truth-check --ci` 10/10 OK with bumped oracle вң….
22. вң… **W152 Wave 13 вҖ” Precision unified at Вұ0.001% + Faza 10.5 acceptance harness + Faza 10.2 fuzz CI + Faza 9.7 throughput report + Faza 14.6 replay differential** вҖ” DONE (this commit). FIVE MASTER_TODO items closed plus precision target tightened **from Вұ0.05% to Вұ0.001%** (50Г— tighter вҖ” operator requirement). Oracle bumped (`ts_test_count ge 2174 вҶ‘ 2130`, `ts_test_files ge 83 вҶ‘ 81`):
   - **Precision unification** вҖ” every Вұ0.05% reference in `SLOT_ENGINE_MASTER_TODO.md` rewritten to Вұ0.001% (1 in 100 000). Cluster (line 165), Faza 10.4 (line 415), Nemerljivi-uspeh В§2. Convergence math documented: at Вұ0.001%/99% target, Пғ=5 (typical slot) вҮ’ N вүҲ 1.66 Г— 10В№ВІ spins (= Faza 9.8 1T territory).
   - **Faza 10.5 acceptance harness** вҖ” `src/sim/acceptanceHarness.ts` (~245 L) implements `requiredSpinsForPrecision()` + `ciHalfWidth()` + `evaluateConvergence()` + `aggregateAcceptance()`. Three acceptance modes: `closed_form` (analytical RTP as reference), `reference_par` (operator-supplied target), `self_replay` (zero-tolerance determinism). 4 ConvergenceStatus outputs: `converged` / `too_few_spins` / `not_converged` / `diverged_from_reference`. Z-scores table for {0.90, 0.95, 0.99, 0.999, 0.9999}. **`scripts/acceptance-dossier.mjs`** (~170 L) consumes the golden snapshot (`reports/acceptance/golden.json`) + optional operator variance map, emits `reports/acceptance/dossier-<UTC>.json` + human-readable `DOSSIER.md` roll-up. 28 vitest tests cover: precision/confidence formula, required-spin scaling, CI half-width, convergence verdict for all 4 statuses + 3 modes + 4 custom configurations, aggregate worst-of, snapshot stability.
   - **Faza 10.2 24h fuzz CI** вҖ” `.github/workflows/fuzz-weekly.yml` weekly Sunday 02:00 UTC cron. 3-target matrix (fuzz_alias / fuzz_eval_config / fuzz_packed_grid) Г— 8h each = 24h total (fits inside GitHub's 24h timeout). Per-target artifact uploads: corpus + crash artifacts + coverage profraw (30-day retention). Fails the job on any crash artifact. Manual dispatch supports `hours_per_target` input.
   - **Faza 9.7 throughput report** вҖ” `reports/bench/THROUGHPUT.md` (~130 L) formalises the вүҘ50M / вүҘ500M / 1T acceptance claims with explicit derivation from `reports/bench/{full_spin,grid_generation,scatter_count,throughput_1M}/*.estimates.json`. Per-thread baselines (2.66M scalar / 4.29M packed M3 Pro), 8-core projection (32M packed Г— 8 вүҲ 256M sustained), GPU scaling factor placeholder, multi-node cluster factor. Acceptance table maps every claim to its current evidence state (measured / projection / pending capture).
   - **Faza 14.6 replay differential** вҖ” `src/replay/longRunDifferential.ts` (~210 L). `buildReplayCapture()` builds a hash-chain checkpoint trail every N spins (default 10 000). `differentialReplay({capture, liveSpinDigests}, todayCommit)` returns 4-state typed outcome: `bit_identical` (same commit + same content), `count_mismatch` (length skew), `checkpoint_mismatch` (with first-divergent-spin pinpoint), `engine_changed_warning` (different commit but same content вҖ” cross-version reproducibility proof). Hash chain construction `H_{i+1} = sha256(H_i || spinDigest_i)` so any tamper propagates to every later digest. 16 vitest tests prove hash-chain non-commutativity, cadence checkpointing, count-mismatch, tamper-detection at next checkpoint, cross-commit warning, zero-spin handling, capture determinism.

   **ULTIMATE QA вҖ” 100% green:** Rust lib 259/259 вң… В· Rust integration 782/782 вң… В· clippy --lib clean вң… В· tsc --noEmit clean вң… В· vitest 2174/2176 (2 intentional skips) вң… В· `npm run build` clean вң… В· `slot-truth-check --ci` 10/10 OK with bumped oracle вң….

## NEMERLJIVI KRITERIJUMI USPEHA

1. **Univerzalnost:** "moЕҫe li config-only da implementira igru X?" вҖ” DA za sve postojeДҮe mehanike (acid-test 30 вң…, nazivni KAT вқҢ).
2. **TaДҚnost:** RTP matuje teoretski sa **Вұ0.001%** na 10вҒ№ spins; PAR sheet match-uje literaturu **Вұ0.001%**. *(W152 Wave 13 вҖ” precision unified at Вұ0.001% (= 1 in 100,000). closed-form вҶ” MC Вұ0.01% вң… na fixture-ima do sada; nightly 10вҒ№-spin acceptance proof za reference fixture-e u `reports/acceptance/`; published PAR cross-validation pending live game audit.)*
3. **Brzina:** вүҘ 500M spins/sec za 5Г—3 lines na M-series single chip; вүҘ 50M za variable-rows ways; GPU вүҘ 50Г— CPU. *(arhitektura postoji; **merenje ne postoji**)*
4. **DeterministiДҚki:** isti config + seed вҶ’ identiДҚan rezultat kroz TS, Rust, GPU. *(TSвҶ”Rust вң…; GPU determinism вҖ” Philox kernel вң…, end-to-end parity вҡ пёҸ)*
5. **Certifiable:** RNG prolazi BigCrush, NIST, PractRand. *(implementacije kanonske вң…; **zvaniДҚni izveЕЎtaji NE postoje**)*
6. **Maintainable:** dodavanje nove mehanike = jedan plugin + jedan test, bez core izmena. *(behavior + feature framework вң…)*
